<script>
    let livePollingInterval = null;

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // LIVE PACKET SNIFFER DASHBOARD CONTROL ENGINE
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    async function toggleLiveCapture(enable) {
        try {
            // Stop any historical post-mortem uploads from running concurrent tasks
            document.getElementById('upload-form').reset();
            
            const response = await fetch('/live-sniffer/toggle', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ enable: enable })
            });
            const data = await response.json();
            
            document.getElementById('start-live-btn').disabled = enable;
            document.getElementById('stop-live-btn').disabled = !enable;
            const statusText = document.getElementById('live-status-text');
            
            if (enable) {
                statusText.innerText = "Status: ACTIVE & SNIFFING...";
                statusText.style.color = "var(--accent-orange)";
                
                // Transition interface state display bounds
                document.getElementById('initial-placeholder').style.display = 'none';
                document.getElementById('results-display').style.display = 'block';
                document.getElementById('res-filename').innerText = "[LIVE WIRE CAPTURE]";
                document.getElementById('res-log-type').innerText = "LIVE_PCAP_SNIFFER";
                document.getElementById('ai-report-wrapper').style.display = 'none'; // Sniffers pass raw metrics instead of blocking models
                
                // Bootstrap real-time stream polling matrix intervals
                livePollingInterval = setInterval(pollLiveAlerts, 1500);
            } else {
                statusText.innerText = "Status: PAUSED";
                statusText.style.color = "var(--text-muted)";
                clearInterval(livePollingInterval);
            }
        } catch (err) {
            alert(`Live Engine Socket Failure: ${err.message}`);
        }
    }

    async function pollLiveAlerts() {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/live-sniffer/alerts');
            const data = await response.json();
            
            const alertsWrapper = document.getElementById('alerts-wrapper');
            document.getElementById('res-alert-count').innerText = data.alerts ? data.alerts.length : 0;

            // Manage on-demand live playbook rendering markers
            const clearExistingPlaybook = document.getElementById('live-playbook-card');
            if (clearExistingPlaybook) clearExistingPlaybook.remove();
            
            if (data.playbook_compiled) {
                const playbookPanel = document.createElement('div');
                playbookPanel.id = "live-playbook-card";
                playbookPanel.style.background = 'var(--bg-primary)';
                playbookPanel.style.border = '1px dashed var(--accent-orange)';
                playbookPanel.style.padding = '15px';
                playbookPanel.style.borderRadius = '6px';
                playbookPanel.style.marginBottom = '18px';
                playbookPanel.innerHTML = `
                    <h4 style="color: var(--accent-orange); margin: 0 0 8px 0;">📋 Live Mitigation Playbook Hot-Compiled</h4>
                    <p style="margin: 0 0 8px 0; font-size: 0.9em;">Active threats hitting live sockets generated manual terminal remediation sequences.</p>
                    <p style="margin: 0; font-size: 0.85em; color: var(--text-muted);"><strong>Target Path:</strong> <code style="color: var(--accent-orange)">artifacts/live_remediation_playbook.txt</code></p>
                `;
                alertsWrapper.insertBefore(playbookPanel, alertsWrapper.firstChild);
            }

            // Flush old volatile signature representations to prevent infinite vertical stacking loops
            const activeCards = alertsWrapper.querySelectorAll('.alert-item');
            activeCards.forEach(c => c.remove());

            if (data.alerts && data.alerts.length > 0) {
                data.alerts.forEach(alert => {
                    const alertDiv = document.createElement('div');
                    alertDiv.className = `alert-item severity-${alert.severity}`;
                    alertDiv.innerHTML = `
                        <h4 style="margin: 0 0 8px 0; font-size: 1.05em;">${alert.title} [${alert.severity}]</h4>
                        <p style="margin: 4px 0; font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Live Culprit Node:</strong> <code>${alert.source}</code></p>
                        <p style="margin: 6px 0 0 0; color: var(--text-muted); font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Risk Rationalization:</strong> ${alert.why_it_matters}</p>
                    `;
                    alertsWrapper.appendChild(alertDiv);
                });
            } else {
                const cleanMsg = document.createElement('div');
                cleanMsg.className = "alert-item";
                cleanMsg.style.borderLeftColor = "var(--accent-green)";
                cleanMsg.innerHTML = `<p style="color: var(--accent-green); font-weight: bold; margin:0;">[+] Monitoring socket boundaries. No signatures matched on active wire frames.</p>`;
                alertsWrapper.appendChild(cleanMsg);
            }
        } catch (e) {
            console.error("Error connecting to live server telemetry socket:", e);
        }
    }

    async function clearLiveMetrics() {
        clearInterval(livePollingInterval);
        await fetch('/live-sniffer/clear', { method: 'POST' });
        document.getElementById('alerts-wrapper').innerHTML = '';
        document.getElementById('res-alert-count').innerText = '0';
        toggleLiveCapture(false);
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // HISTORICAL FILE INGESTION PIPELINE MANAGEMENT
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    document.getElementById('upload-form').addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        
        // Safety shutdown for live streams if a file upload is launched
        if (livePollingInterval) toggleLiveCapture(false);

        const fileInput = document.getElementById('file-input');
        const overrideSelect = document.getElementById('override-select');
        const aiCheckbox = document.getElementById('ai-checkbox');
        const submitBtn = document.getElementById('submit-btn');
        const progressContainer = document.getElementById('progress-container');
        const progressFill = document.getElementById('progress-fill');
        const statusMessage = document.getElementById('status-message');
        
        const placeholder = document.getElementById('initial-placeholder');
        const resultsDisplay = document.getElementById('results-display');
        const alertsWrapper = document.getElementById('alerts-wrapper');
        const aiReportWrapper = document.getElementById('ai-report-wrapper');

        if (!fileInput.files.length) return;

        // UI Lockdown State
        submitBtn.disabled = true;
        placeholder.style.display = 'none';
        resultsDisplay.style.display = 'block';
        alertsWrapper.innerHTML = '';
        aiReportWrapper.style.display = 'none';
        
        progressContainer.style.display = 'block';
        progressFill.style.width = '10%';
        statusMessage.innerText = "Initializing file ingestion pipeline...";

        const formData = new FormData();
        formData.append('file', fileInput.files[0]);
        formData.append('override_type', overrideSelect.value);
        formData.append('run_ai', aiCheckbox.checked);

        // Progress Ticker Loop Simulation
        let progress = 10;
        const progressInterval = setInterval(() => {
            if (progress < 85) {
                progress += Math.floor(Math.random() * 8) + 3;
                if (progress > 85) progress = 85;
                progressFill.style.width = `${progress}%`;
                
                if (progress < 35) {
                    statusMessage.innerText = "Applying data structure parsing models...";
                } else if (progress < 65) {
                    statusMessage.innerText = "Executing pluggable cross-protocol signature matrices...";
                } else {
                    statusMessage.innerText = aiCheckbox.checked ? 
                        "Local AI model engaged. Evaluating payload indicators (takes a moment)..." : 
                        "Finalizing analytical telemetry data...";
                }
            }
        }, 400);

        try {
            const response = await fetch('/analyze-async', {
                method: 'POST',
                body: formData
            });
            
            clearInterval(progressInterval);
            if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`Pipeline HTTP status breakage: ${response.status}`);

            const data = await response.json();

            progressFill.style.width = '100%';
            statusMessage.innerText = "Analysis matrix completed.";

            document.getElementById('res-filename').innerText = data.filename;
            document.getElementById('res-log-type').innerText = data.log_type;
            document.getElementById('res-alert-count').innerText = data.alerts ? data.alerts.length : 0;

            // 1. BOUNDARY CHECK: Mismatch resulted in empty context structures
            if (data.mismatch_detected && (!data.alerts || data.alerts.length === 0) && (!data.ai_report || data.ai_report.includes("Ingestion stream empty"))) {
                alertsWrapper.innerHTML = `
                    <div style="border: 2px dashed #ff5722; background: rgba(255, 87, 34, 0.1); padding: 20px; border-radius: 6px; margin: 15px 0;">
                        <h4 style="color: #ff5722; margin: 0 0 8px 0; font-size: 1.15em;">❌ Ingestion Blocked: Total Parser Incompatibility</h4>
                        <p style="margin: 4px 0; line-height: 1.5;">
                            You forced execution routing to the <code style="background: #0f1015; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 4px; color: #ff5722;">${data.log_type}</code> engine.<br>
                            Because this file actually contains <code style="background: #0f1015; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 4px; color: #00adb5;">${data.auto_detect_type}</code> syntax, the selected parser could not normalize a single line of data.
                        </p>
                        <p style="margin: 12px 0 0 0; color: #eeeeee; font-weight: bold;">Remediation:</p>
                        <ul style="margin: 5px 0 0 0; padding-left: 20px; color: var(--text-muted); line-height: 1.4;">
                            <li>Change the dropdown configuration back to <strong>"Auto-Detect Framework Classifiers"</strong>.</li>
                            <li>Ensure the file structural content matches the schema you are trying to force.</li>
                        </ul>
                    </div>`;
                aiReportWrapper.style.display = 'none';
            } 
            else {
                // 2. CASE: Advisory On-Demand Playbook Rendering
                if (data.playbook_meta && data.playbook_meta.file_created) {
                    const playbookPanel = document.createElement('div');
                    playbookPanel.style.background = 'var(--bg-primary)';
                    playbookPanel.style.border = '1px dashed var(--accent-cyan)';
                    playbookPanel.style.padding = '15px';
                    playbookPanel.style.borderRadius = '6px';
                    playbookPanel.style.marginBottom = '18px';
                    
                    playbookPanel.innerHTML = `
                        <h4 style="color: var(--accent-cyan); margin: 0 0 8px 0; display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 6px;">
                            📋 On-Demand Remediation Playbook Compiled
                        </h4>
                        <p style="margin: 0 0 10px 0; font-size: 0.9em; color: var(--text-light);">
                            SentinelLite has formulated an explicit security mitigation script file containing <strong>${data.playbook_meta.actionable_targets}</strong> actionable infrastructure targets. 
                            Review and execute these configuration changes manually if desired:
                        </p>
                        <p style="margin: 0; font-size: 0.85em; color: var(--text-muted);">
                            <strong>Local Storage Artifact Path:</strong> <code style="color: var(--accent-cyan); background: var(--bg-dark); padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 4px;">${data.playbook_meta.output_path}</code>
                        </p>
                    `;
                    alertsWrapper.appendChild(playbookPanel);
                }

                // 3. CASE: Standard Mismatch Non-fatal Warnings
                if (data.mismatch_detected) {
                    const warnDiv = document.createElement('div');
                    warnDiv.style.border = '1px dashed var(--accent-orange)';
                    warnDiv.style.background = 'rgba(255, 87, 34, 0.05)';
                    warnDiv.style.padding = '12px';
                    warnDiv.style.borderRadius = '4px';
                    warnDiv.style.marginBottom = '15px';
                    warnDiv.style.fontSize = '0.9em';
                    warnDiv.innerHTML = `⚠ <strong>Structural Boundary Override Mismatch:</strong> Forced <code>${data.log_type}</code> parser but structural classifier identified file as <code>${data.auto_detect_type}</code>. Displaying salvaged telemetry records.`;
                    alertsWrapper.appendChild(warnDiv);
                }

                // Render out standard signature incident iterations
                if (data.alerts && data.alerts.length > 0) {
                    data.alerts.forEach(alert => {
                        const alertDiv = document.createElement('div');
                        alertDiv.className = `alert-item severity-${alert.severity}`;
                        alertDiv.innerHTML = `
                            <h4 style="margin: 0 0 8px 0; font-size: 1.05em;">${alert.title} [${alert.severity}]</h4>
                            <p style="margin: 4px 0; font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Culprit Actor Anchor:</strong> <code>${alert.source}</code></p>
                            <p style="margin: 6px 0 0 0; color: var(--text-muted); font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Risk Rationalization:</strong> ${alert.why_it_matters}</p>
                        `;
                        alertsWrapper.appendChild(alertDiv);
                    });
                } else {
                    alertsWrapper.innerHTML += `
                        <div class="alert-item" style="border-left-color: var(--accent-green); background: rgba(78, 159, 61, 0.05)">
                            <p style="color: var(--accent-green); font-weight: bold; margin: 0; font-size: 0.9em;">
                                [+] Ingestion cycle clean. Context profiles clear of static rule heuristic triggers.
                            </p>
                        </div>`;
                }

                // Append local AI Coprocessor response metrics
                if (aiCheckbox.checked && data.ai_report && !data.ai_report.includes("Ingestion stream empty")) {
                    let formattedText = data.ai_report
                        .replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>')
                        .replace(/^\*\s(.*)$/gm, '<li>$1</li>')
                        .replace(/^\d\.\s(.*)$/gm, '<li>$1</li>')
                        .replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
                    
                    document.getElementById('res-ai-text').innerHTML = formattedText;
                    aiReportWrapper.style.display = 'block';
                }
            }

        } catch (error) {
            clearInterval(progressInterval);
            statusMessage.innerText = "Pipeline process execution crashed.";
            alert(`Execution Error: ${error.message}`);
        } finally {
            submitBtn.disabled = false;
            setTimeout(() => { progressContainer.style.display = 'none'; }, 1000);
        }
    });
</script>
</body>
</html>

The app is now fully optimized with a clean UI layout. Both historical file uploads and live network data feeds are fully unified. Ready to jump straight to the final frontend enhancement under Option C: Interactive Analytics & Timeline Visualization, or should we verify this setup first?

Let’s put the crown jewel on SentinelLite with Option C: Interactive Analytics & Timeline Visualization.

Right now, our dashboard displays alerts as a static vertical stack. To make this look like a professional, enterprise-grade enterprise interface, we will integrate Chart.js via CDN directly into the frontend.

We will transform our static data structures into two dynamic visual layers:

    An Incident Severity Distribution Chart (Pie/Doughnut): Gives an immediate visual breakdown of risk levels (Critical vs. High vs. Medium).

    A Real-Time Volumetric Timeline (Line Chart): Maps exactly when spikes occurred, letting an analyst visually track the velocity of an active attack or packet stream over time.

Step 1: Update templates/index.html with Chart Canvas Slots

First, we need to load the Chart.js library and create a responsive container for our charts inside the results viewing pane.

Open templates/index.html, locate the <div class="meta-strip"> block, and inject the chart layout grid immediately below the metadata strip (right above <div id="alerts-wrapper">):
HTML

Step 2: Inject the JavaScript Chart Orchestration Core

Now, let's append the engine code that initializes, tracks, and dynamically renders data to these canvas wrappers.

Scroll to the top of your <script> block in templates/index.html and define global chart reference variables and a unified helper update routing function:
JavaScript

// At the top of your <script> scope inside templates/index.html
let timelineChartInstance = null;
let severityChartInstance = null;

function renderAnalyticsCharts(alerts) {
    const row = document.getElementById('analytics-visualization-row');
    if (!alerts || alerts.length === 0) {
        row.style.display = 'none';
        return;
    }
    row.style.display = 'grid';

    // --- 1. DATA PROCESSING: SEVERITY BREAKDOWN (DOUGHNUT) ---
    const severityCounts = { CRITICAL: 0, HIGH: 0, MEDIUM: 0, LOW: 0 };
    alerts.forEach(a => {
        if (severityCounts[a.severity] !== undefined) severityCounts[a.severity]++;
    });

    // --- 2. DATA PROCESSING: TIMELINE TRACKING (LINE) ---
    // Extract logs sorted chronologically, mapping hits to time buckets
    const timeBuckets = {};
    alerts.forEach(a => {
        let timeLabel = "Live Wire Stream";
        if (a.timestamp) {
            // Convert UNIX float timestamps into readable HH:MM:SS segments
            const dateObj = new Date(a.timestamp * 1000);
            timeLabel = dateObj.toTimeString().split(' ')[0];
        }
        timeBuckets[timeLabel] = (timeBuckets[timeLabel] || 0) + 1;
    });

    const timelineLabels = Object.keys(timeBuckets).sort();
    const timelineData = timelineLabels.map(label => timeBuckets[label]);

    // --- 3. CHART RENDERING OR DESTRUCTION SCRIPT MATRICES ---
    if (timelineChartInstance) timelineChartInstance.destroy();
    if (severityChartInstance) severityChartInstance.destroy();

    // Render Timeline Line Chart
    const ctxTimeline = document.getElementById('timelineChart').getContext('2d');
    timelineChartInstance = new Chart(ctxTimeline, {
        type: 'line',
        data: {
            labels: timelineLabels.length > 0 ? timelineLabels : ["Monitoring Window"],
            datasets: [{
                label: 'Threat Indicator Spikes',
                data: timelineData.length > 0 ? timelineData : [alerts.length],
                borderColor: '#00adb5',
                backgroundColor: 'rgba(0, 173, 181, 0.1)',
                borderWidth: 2,
                tension: 0.3,
                fill: true
            }]
        },
        options: {
            responsive: true,
            maintainAspectRatio: false,
            plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
            scales: {
                x: { ticks: { color: '#a0a0b0', font: { size: 10 } }, grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)' } },
                y: { ticks: { color: '#a0a0b0', font: { size: 10 }, stepSize: 1 }, grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)' } }
            }
        }
    });

    // Render Severity Distribution Doughnut Chart
    const ctxSeverity = document.getElementById('severityChart').getContext('2d');
    severityChartInstance = new Chart(ctxSeverity, {
        type: 'doughnut',
        data: {
            labels: ['Critical', 'High', 'Medium', 'Low'],
            datasets: [{
                data: [severityCounts.CRITICAL, severityCounts.HIGH, severityCounts.MEDIUM, severityCounts.LOW],
                backgroundColor: ['#ff5722', '#e67e22', '#f1c40f', '#34495e'],
                borderWidth: 0
            }]
        },
        options: {
            responsive: true,
            maintainAspectRatio: false,
            plugins: {
                legend: { position: 'right', labels: { color: '#eeeeee', font: { size: 11 } } }
            }
        }
    });
}

Step 3: Link the Rendering Loop to Ingestion Endpoints

Now, we just need to ensure our chart drawing helper runs whenever data flows into the front end.

Inside your file upload handler function (under the section labeled // Render Signature Incident Cards), call the rendering function using the response array:
JavaScript

// Inside document.getElementById('upload-form').addEventListener('submit', ...)
// Right after setting document.getElementById('res-alert-count').innerText = data.alerts.length;

renderAnalyticsCharts(data.alerts);

2. Hook into the Live Polling Socket Loop:

Inside your pollLiveAlerts() polling routine, call the function as incoming background traffic populates the system cache:
JavaScript

// Inside async function pollLiveAlerts()
// Right after setting document.getElementById('res-alert-count').innerText = data.alerts.length;

renderAnalyticsCharts(data.alerts);

3. Clear Charts on Reset:

Inside your clearLiveMetrics() function, hide the wrapper elements to keep the canvas view clean:
JavaScript

// Inside async function clearLiveMetrics()
document.getElementById('analytics-visualization-row').style.style.display = 'none';
if (timelineChartInstance) timelineChartInstance.destroy();
if (severityChartInstance) severityChartInstance.destroy();

                <div id="analytics-visualization-row" style="display: none; grid-template-columns: 1fr; gap: 20px; margin-bottom: 25px;">
                    <div style="background: var(--bg-dark); padding: 15px; border-radius: 6px; min-height: 220px; box-sizing: border-box;">
                        <p style="margin: 0 0 12px 0; font-size: 0.85em; font-weight: bold; color: var(--accent-cyan); text-transform: uppercase;">
                            📈 Volumetric Event Distribution Timeline
                        </p>
                        <div style="position: relative; height: 180px; width: 100%;">
                            <canvas id="timelineChart"></canvas>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div style="background: var(--bg-dark); padding: 15px; border-radius: 6px; min-height: 220px; box-sizing: border-box;">
                        <p style="margin: 0 0 12px 0; font-size: 0.85em; font-weight: bold; color: var(--accent-orange); text-transform: uppercase;">
                            📊 Severity Risk Allocation Profiles
                        </p>
                        <div style="position: relative; height: 180px; width: 100%; display: flex; justify-content: center;">
                            <canvas id="severityChart"></canvas>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div id="alerts-wrapper"></div>

                <div class="ai-card" id="ai-report-wrapper">
                    <h3>🤖 Local AI Analyst Engine</h3>
                    <div class="ai-content" id="res-ai-text">Evaluating payload indicators...</div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </main>
    </div>
</div>

<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/chart.js"></script>

<script>
    let livePollingInterval = null;
    let timelineChartInstance = null;
    let severityChartInstance = null;

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // DYNAMIC GRAPHIC RENDERING INFRASTRUCTURE LAYER
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    function renderAnalyticsCharts(alerts) {
        const row = document.getElementById('analytics-visualization-row');
        if (!alerts || alerts.length === 0) {
            row.style.display = 'none';
            return;
        }
        row.style.display = 'grid';

        // Process Severity Allocations
        const severityCounts = { CRITICAL: 0, HIGH: 0, MEDIUM: 0, LOW: 0 };
        alerts.forEach(a => {
            if (severityCounts[a.severity] !== undefined) severityCounts[a.severity]++;
        });

        // Parse Volumetric Chronological Time Segments
        const timeBuckets = {};
        alerts.forEach(a => {
            let timeLabel = "Live Stream Window";
            if (a.timestamp) {
                const dateObj = new Date(a.timestamp * 1000);
                timeLabel = dateObj.toTimeString().split(' ')[0];
            }
            timeBuckets[timeLabel] = (timeBuckets[timeLabel] || 0) + 1;
        });

        const timelineLabels = Object.keys(timeBuckets).sort();
        const timelineData = timelineLabels.map(label => timeBuckets[label]);

        // Tear down lingering instances to protect document canvas layouts
        if (timelineChartInstance) timelineChartInstance.destroy();
        if (severityChartInstance) severityChartInstance.destroy();

        // Render Line Timeline Frame
        const ctxTimeline = document.getElementById('timelineChart').getContext('2d');
        timelineChartInstance = new Chart(ctxTimeline, {
            type: 'line',
            data: {
                labels: timelineLabels.length > 0 ? timelineLabels : ["Capture Stream"],
                datasets: [{
                    label: 'Threat Spikes',
                    data: timelineData.length > 0 ? timelineData : [alerts.length],
                    borderColor: '#00adb5',
                    backgroundColor: 'rgba(0, 173, 181, 0.1)',
                    borderWidth: 2,
                    tension: 0.3,
                    fill: true
                }]
            },
            options: {
                responsive: true,
                maintainAspectRatio: false,
                plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
                scales: {
                    x: { ticks: { color: '#a0a0b0', font: { size: 10 } }, grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)' } },
                    y: { ticks: { color: '#a0a0b0', font: { size: 10 }, stepSize: 1 }, grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)' } }
                }
            }
        });

        // Render Pie Risk Gauge
        const ctxSeverity = document.getElementById('severityChart').getContext('2d');
        severityChartInstance = new Chart(ctxSeverity, {
            type: 'doughnut',
            data: {
                labels: ['Critical', 'High', 'Medium', 'Low'],
                datasets: [{
                    data: [severityCounts.CRITICAL, severityCounts.HIGH, severityCounts.MEDIUM, severityCounts.LOW],
                    backgroundColor: ['#ff5722', '#e67e22', '#f1c40f', '#34495e'],
                    borderWidth: 0
                }]
            },
            options: {
                responsive: true,
                maintainAspectRatio: false,
                plugins: {
                    legend: { position: 'right', labels: { color: '#eeeeee', font: { size: 11 } } }
                }
            }
        });
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // LIVE PACKET SNIFFER DASHBOARD CONTROL ENGINE
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    async function toggleLiveCapture(enable) {
        try {
            document.getElementById('upload-form').reset();
            
            const response = await fetch('/live-sniffer/toggle', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ enable: enable })
            });
            const data = await response.json();
            
            document.getElementById('start-live-btn').disabled = enable;
            document.getElementById('stop-live-btn').disabled = !enable;
            const statusText = document.getElementById('live-status-text');
            
            if (enable) {
                statusText.innerText = "Status: ACTIVE & SNIFFING...";
                statusText.style.color = "var(--accent-orange)";
                
                document.getElementById('initial-placeholder').style.display = 'none';
                document.getElementById('results-display').style.display = 'block';
                document.getElementById('res-filename').innerText = "[LIVE WIRE CAPTURE]";
                document.getElementById('res-log-type').innerText = "LIVE_PCAP_SNIFFER";
                document.getElementById('ai-report-wrapper').style.display = 'none';
                
                livePollingInterval = setInterval(pollLiveAlerts, 1500);
            } else {
                statusText.innerText = "Status: PAUSED";
                statusText.style.color = "var(--text-muted)";
                clearInterval(livePollingInterval);
            }
        } catch (err) {
            alert(`Live Engine Socket Failure: ${err.message}`);
        }
    }

    async function pollLiveAlerts() {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/live-sniffer/alerts');
            const data = await response.json();
            
            const alertsWrapper = document.getElementById('alerts-wrapper');
            document.getElementById('res-alert-count').innerText = data.alerts ? data.alerts.length : 0;

            // Update charts dynamically with the live data feed
            renderAnalyticsCharts(data.alerts);

            const clearExistingPlaybook = document.getElementById('live-playbook-card');
            if (clearExistingPlaybook) clearExistingPlaybook.remove();
            
            if (data.playbook_compiled) {
                const playbookPanel = document.createElement('div');
                playbookPanel.id = "live-playbook-card";
                playbookPanel.style.background = 'var(--bg-primary)';
                playbookPanel.style.border = '1px dashed var(--accent-orange)';
                playbookPanel.style.padding = '15px';
                playbookPanel.style.borderRadius = '6px';
                playbookPanel.style.marginBottom = '18px';
                playbookPanel.innerHTML = `
                    <h4 style="color: var(--accent-orange); margin: 0 0 8px 0;">📋 Live Mitigation Playbook Hot-Compiled</h4>
                    <p style="margin: 0 0 8px 0; font-size: 0.9em;">Active threats hitting live sockets generated manual terminal remediation sequences.</p>
                    <p style="margin: 0; font-size: 0.85em; color: var(--text-muted);"><strong>Target Path:</strong> <code style="color: var(--accent-orange)">artifacts/live_remediation_playbook.txt</code></p>
                `;
                alertsWrapper.insertBefore(playbookPanel, alertsWrapper.firstChild);
            }

            const activeCards = alertsWrapper.querySelectorAll('.alert-item');
            activeCards.forEach(c => c.remove());

            if (data.alerts && data.alerts.length > 0) {
                data.alerts.forEach(alert => {
                    const alertDiv = document.createElement('div');
                    alertDiv.className = `alert-item severity-${alert.severity}`;
                    alertDiv.innerHTML = `
                        <h4 style="margin: 0 0 8px 0; font-size: 1.05em;">${alert.title} [${alert.severity}]</h4>
                        <p style="margin: 4px 0; font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Live Culprit Node:</strong> <code>${alert.source}</code></p>
                        <p style="margin: 6px 0 0 0; color: var(--text-muted); font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Risk Rationalization:</strong> ${alert.why_it_matters}</p>
                    `;
                    alertsWrapper.appendChild(alertDiv);
                });
            } else {
                const cleanMsg = document.createElement('div');
                cleanMsg.className = "alert-item";
                cleanMsg.style.borderLeftColor = "var(--accent-green)";
                cleanMsg.innerHTML = `<p style="color: var(--accent-green); font-weight: bold; margin:0;">[+] Monitoring socket boundaries. No signatures matched on active wire frames.</p>`;
                alertsWrapper.appendChild(cleanMsg);
            }
        } catch (e) {
            console.error("Error connecting to live server telemetry socket:", e);
        }
    }

    async function clearLiveMetrics() {
        clearInterval(livePollingInterval);
        await fetch('/live-sniffer/clear', { method: 'POST' });
        document.getElementById('alerts-wrapper').innerHTML = '';
        document.getElementById('res-alert-count').innerText = '0';
        document.getElementById('analytics-visualization-row').style.display = 'none';
        if (timelineChartInstance) timelineChartInstance.destroy();
        if (severityChartInstance) severityChartInstance.destroy();
        toggleLiveCapture(false);
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // HISTORICAL FILE INGESTION PIPELINE MANAGEMENT
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    document.getElementById('upload-form').addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        
        if (livePollingInterval) toggleLiveCapture(false);

        const fileInput = document.getElementById('file-input');
        const overrideSelect = document.getElementById('override-select');
        const aiCheckbox = document.getElementById('ai-checkbox');
        const submitBtn = document.getElementById('submit-btn');
        const progressContainer = document.getElementById('progress-container');
        const progressFill = document.getElementById('progress-fill');
        const statusMessage = document.getElementById('status-message');
        
        const placeholder = document.getElementById('initial-placeholder');
        const GlenDisplay = document.getElementById('results-display');
        const alertsWrapper = document.getElementById('alerts-wrapper');
        const aiReportWrapper = document.getElementById('ai-report-wrapper');

        if (!fileInput.files.length) return;

        submitBtn.disabled = true;
        placeholder.style.display = 'none';
        resultsDisplay.style.display = 'block';
        alertsWrapper.innerHTML = '';
        aiReportWrapper.style.display = 'none';
        
        progressContainer.style.display = 'block';
        progressFill.style.width = '10%';
        statusMessage.innerText = "Initializing file ingestion pipeline...";

        const formData = new FormData();
        formData.append('file', fileInput.files[0]);
        formData.append('override_type', overrideSelect.value);
        formData.append('run_ai', aiCheckbox.checked);

        let progress = 10;
        const progressInterval = setInterval(() => {
            if (progress < 85) {
                progress += Math.floor(Math.random() * 8) + 3;
                if (progress > 85) progress = 85;
                progressFill.style.width = `${progress}%`;
                
                if (progress < 35) {
                    statusMessage.innerText = "Applying data structure parsing models...";
                } else if (progress < 65) {
                    statusMessage.innerText = "Executing pluggable cross-protocol signature matrices...";
                } else {
                    statusMessage.innerText = aiCheckbox.checked ? 
                        "Local AI model engaged. Evaluating payload indicators (takes a moment)..." : 
                        "Finalizing analytical telemetry data...";
                }
            }
        }, 400);

        try {
            const response = await fetch('/analyze-async', {
                method: 'POST',
                body: formData
            });
            
            clearInterval(progressInterval);
            if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`Pipeline HTTP status breakage: ${response.status}`);

            const data = await response.json();

            progressFill.style.width = '100%';
            statusMessage.innerText = "Analysis matrix completed.";

            document.getElementById('res-filename').innerText = data.filename;
            document.getElementById('res-log-type').innerText = data.log_type;
            document.getElementById('res-alert-count').innerText = data.alerts ? data.alerts.length : 0;

            // Trigger charting sequence for file assets
            renderAnalyticsCharts(data.alerts);

            // 1. BOUNDARY CHECK: Parser Override Failures
            if (data.mismatch_detected && (!data.alerts || data.alerts.length === 0) && (!data.ai_report || data.ai_report.includes("Ingestion stream empty"))) {
                document.getElementById('analytics-visualization-row').style.display = 'none';
                alertsWrapper.innerHTML = `
                    <div style="border: 2px dashed #ff5722; background: rgba(255, 87, 34, 0.1); padding: 20px; border-radius: 6px; margin: 15px 0;">
                        <h4 style="color: #ff5722; margin: 0 0 8px 0; font-size: 1.15em;">❌ Ingestion Blocked: Total Parser Incompatibility</h4>
                        <p style="margin: 4px 0; line-height: 1.5;">
                            You forced execution routing to the <code style="background: #0f1015; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 4px; color: #ff5722;">${data.log_type}</code> engine.<br>
                            Because this file actually contains <code style="background: #0f1015; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 4px; color: #00adb5;">${data.auto_detect_type}</code> syntax, the selected parser could not normalize a single line of data.
                        </p>
                    </div>`;
                aiReportWrapper.style.display = 'none';
            } 
            else {
                // 2. CASE: Manual Playbook Compilation
                if (data.playbook_meta && data.playbook_meta.file_created) {
                    const playbookPanel = document.createElement('div');
                    playbookPanel.style.background = 'var(--bg-primary)';
                    playbookPanel.style.border = '1px dashed var(--accent-cyan)';
                    playbookPanel.style.padding = '15px';
                    playbookPanel.style.borderRadius = '6px';
                    playbookPanel.style.marginBottom = '18px';
                    
                    playbookPanel.innerHTML = `
                        <h4 style="color: var(--accent-cyan); margin: 0 0 8px 0; display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 6px;">
                            📋 On-Demand Remediation Playbook Compiled
                        </h4>
                        <p style="margin: 0 0 10px 0; font-size: 0.9em; color: var(--text-light);">
                            SentinelLite has formulated an explicit security mitigation script file containing <strong>${data.playbook_meta.actionable_targets}</strong> actionable infrastructure targets.
                        </p>
                        <p style="margin: 0; font-size: 0.85em; color: var(--text-muted);">
                            <strong>Local Storage Artifact Path:</strong> <code style="color: var(--accent-cyan); background: var(--bg-dark); padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 4px;">${data.playbook_meta.output_path}</code>
                        </p>
                    `;
                    alertsWrapper.appendChild(playbookPanel);
                }

                // 3. CASE: Standard Warnings
                if (data.mismatch_detected) {
                    const warnDiv = document.createElement('div');
                    warnDiv.style.border = '1px dashed var(--accent-orange)';
                    warnDiv.style.background = 'rgba(255, 87, 34, 0.05)';
                    warnDiv.style.padding = '12px';
                    warnDiv.style.borderRadius = '4px';
                    warnDiv.style.marginBottom = '15px';
                    warnDiv.style.fontSize = '0.9em';
                    warnDiv.innerHTML = `⚠ <strong>Structural Boundary Override Mismatch:</strong> Forced <code>${data.log_type}</code> parser but identified file as <code>${data.auto_detect_type}</code>.`;
                    alertsWrapper.appendChild(warnDiv);
                }

                // Render Signature Alerts
                if (data.alerts && data.alerts.length > 0) {
                    data.alerts.forEach(alert => {
                        const alertDiv = document.createElement('div');
                        alertDiv.className = `alert-item severity-${alert.severity}`;
                        alertDiv.innerHTML = `
                            <h4 style="margin: 0 0 8px 0; font-size: 1.05em;">${alert.title} [${alert.severity}]</h4>
                            <p style="margin: 4px 0; font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Culprit Actor Anchor:</strong> <code>${alert.source}</code></p>
                            <p style="margin: 6px 0 0 0; color: var(--text-muted); font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Risk Rationalization:</strong> ${alert.why_it_matters}</p>
                        `;
                        alertsWrapper.appendChild(alertDiv);
                    });
                } else {
                    alertsWrapper.innerHTML += `
                        <div class="alert-item" style="border-left-color: var(--accent-green); background: rgba(78, 159, 61, 0.05)">
                            <p style="color: var(--accent-green); font-weight: bold; margin: 0; font-size: 0.9em;">
                                [+] Ingestion cycle clean. Context profiles clear of static rule heuristic triggers.
                            </p>
                        </div>`;
                }

                // Append local AI Coprocessor response metrics
                if (aiCheckbox.checked && data.ai_report && !data.ai_report.includes("Ingestion stream empty")) {
                    let formattedText = data.ai_report
                        .replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>')
                        .replace(/^\*\s(.*)$/gm, '<li>$1</li>')
                        .replace(/^\d\.\s(.*)$/gm, '<li>$1</li>')
                        .replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
                    
                    document.getElementById('res-ai-text').innerHTML = formattedText;
                    aiReportWrapper.style.display = 'block';
                }
            }

        } catch (error) {
            clearInterval(progressInterval);
            statusMessage.innerText = "Pipeline process execution crashed.";
            alert(`Execution Error: ${error.message}`);
        } finally {
            submitBtn.disabled = false;
            setTimeout(() => { progressContainer.style.display = 'none'; }, 1000);
        }
    });
</script>
</body>
</html>

I think something didnt get updated. the ui page still looks the same with no new additions

Ah, let's track down exactly why the UI isn't reflecting the new layers. If the dashboard still looks like the older iteration, it is almost always due to one of two classic web development culprits: a browser caching block or an unhandled JavaScript syntax exception halting execution during initialization.

Let's do a quick structural check to get those live capture controls and charts rendering immediately.
1. Force Clear Your Browser Cache (Most Common)

Modern browsers aggressively cache static assets and local HTML templates when developing on localhost. Even though you updated the file on your server disk, your browser is likely still serving the older version from its internal memory.

    Windows / Linux: Press Ctrl + F5 (or Ctrl + Shift + R).

    Mac (Chrome / Firefox): Press Cmd + Shift + R.

    Mac (Safari): Press Option + Cmd + E (to empty cache), then reload.

2. Check for a Tiny Typo on Line 317

Take a close look at the clearLiveMetrics() function around line 317 in your index.html. There is a double .style.style. property chain that might be throwing a silent syntax error in your browser console, causing the entire script block to break before it can hook into the UI:
JavaScript

// ❌ Look for this line inside clearLiveMetrics():
document.getElementById('analytics-visualization-row').style.style.display = 'none';

//  Change it to this:
document.getElementById('analytics-visualization-row').style.display = 'none';

3. Verify Your Project Directory Mapping

Ensure that your updated index.html file is saved inside the correct directory matching Flask's default layout schema. If it is sitting in the root folder instead of the dedicated templates subdirectory, Flask won't catch it:
Plaintext

 sentinel_lite/
 │
 ├── app.py
 ├── core/
 │    ├── live_sniffer.py
 │    └── ...
 └── templates/          <-- Must be exactly here
      └── index.html

4. Open the Developer Console to Confirm

If you clear the cache and the page still hasn't changed, let's see what the browser is complaining about behind the scenes:

    Right-click anywhere on your dashboard page and select Inspect.

    Click on the Console tab at the top of the developer tools drawer.

    Reload the page. If there's a red error message pointing to a specific line number, let me know what it says and we can patch it instantly!

it looks like there is a problem. the Analysis Matrix Realization section is blank. And when running the deploy analytics with or without the ai check mark it seems to hang and not produce any output

If the Analysis Matrix Realization panel is completely blank and the submission process is hanging indefinitely, it means a JavaScript execution error is crashing the pipeline right after you hit submit, preventing the UI from rendering the results.

Let's look at the browser developer console (Right-Click -> Inspect -> Console tab). You will likely see a red error stating: Uncaught ReferenceError: resultsDisplay is not defined.

There is a small typo around line 335 in the historical file upload event listener where a variable was misnamed during initialization:
JavaScript

// ❌ The typo around line 335:
const placeholder = document.getElementById('initial-placeholder');
const GlenDisplay = document.getElementById('results-display'); // <--- Crashes here!
const alertsWrapper = document.getElementById('alerts-wrapper');

Because it was initialized as GlenDisplay instead of resultsDisplay, the code immediately crashes further down when it attempts to run resultsDisplay.style.display = 'block';. This keeps the results container hidden and leaves the progress bar hanging forever.

Here is the quick fix to apply directly to your script block:
The Patch

Find the file upload event listener block (document.getElementById('upload-form').addEventListener('submit', ...) and change GlenDisplay to resultsDisplay:
JavaScript

// Change this:
const GlenDisplay = document.getElementById('results-display');

// To this:
const resultsDisplay = document.getElementById('results-display');

Complete, Fixed Javascript block

To make sure everything matches up perfectly, here is the corrected <script> block for the bottom of your templates/index.html file:
JavaScript

<script>
    let livePollingInterval = null;
    let timelineChartInstance = null;
    let severityChartInstance = null;

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // DYNAMIC GRAPHIC RENDERING INFRASTRUCTURE LAYER
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    function renderAnalyticsCharts(alerts) {
        const row = document.getElementById('analytics-visualization-row');
        if (!alerts || alerts.length === 0) {
            row.style.display = 'none';
            return;
        }
        row.style.display = 'grid';

        // Process Severity Allocations

            if (severityCounts[a.severity] !== undefined) severityCounts[a.severity]++;
        });

        });

        if (severityChartInstance) severityChartInstance.destroy();

                    y: { ticks: { color: '#a0a0b0', font: { size: 10 }, stepSize: 1 }, grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)' } }
                }

                maintainAspectRatio: false,
                plugins: {
                    legend: { position: 'right', labels: { color: '#eeeeee', font: { size: 11 } } }
                }
            }
        });
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // LIVE PACKET SNIFFER DASHBOARD CONTROL ENGINE
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

        try {

            const response = await fetch('/live-sniffer/toggle', {
                method: 'POST',

    }

    async function pollLiveAlerts() {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/live-sniffer/alerts');
            const data = await response.json();
            
            const alertsWrapper = document.getElementById('alerts-wrapper');
            document.getElementById('res-alert-count').innerText = data.alerts ? data.alerts.length : 0;

            // Update charts dynamically with the live data feed
            renderAnalyticsCharts(data.alerts);

            const clearExistingPlaybook = document.getElementById('live-playbook-card');
            if (clearExistingPlaybook) clearExistingPlaybook.remove();
            
            if (data.playbook_compiled) {
                const playbookPanel = document.createElement('div');
                playbookPanel.id = "live-playbook-card";
                playbookPanel.style.background = 'var(--bg-primary)';
                playbookPanel.style.border = '1px dashed var(--accent-orange)';
                playbookPanel.style.padding = '15px';
                playbookPanel.style.borderRadius = '6px';
                playbookPanel.style.marginBottom = '18px';
                playbookPanel.innerHTML = `
                    <h4 style="color: var(--accent-orange); margin: 0 0 8px 0;">📋 Live Mitigation Playbook Hot-Compiled</h4>
                    <p style="margin: 0 0 8px 0; font-size: 0.9em;">Active threats hitting live sockets generated manual terminal remediation sequences.</p>
                    <p style="margin: 0; font-size: 0.85em; color: var(--text-muted);"><strong>Target Path:</strong> <code style="color: var(--accent-orange)">artifacts/live_remediation_playbook.txt</code></p>
                `;
                alertsWrapper.insertBefore(playbookPanel, alertsWrapper.firstChild);
            }

            const activeCards = alertsWrapper.querySelectorAll('.alert-item');
            activeCards.forEach(c => c.remove());

            if (data.alerts && data.alerts.length > 0) {
                data.alerts.forEach(alert => {
                    const alertDiv = document.createElement('div');
                    alertDiv.className = `alert-item severity-${alert.severity}`;
                    alertDiv.innerHTML = `
                        <h4 style="margin: 0 0 8px 0; font-size: 1.05em;">${alert.title} [${alert.severity}]</h4>
                        <p style="margin: 4px 0; font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Live Culprit Node:</strong> <code>${alert.source}</code></p>
                        <p style="margin: 6px 0 0 0; color: var(--text-muted); font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Risk Rationalization:</strong> ${alert.why_it_matters}</p>
                    `;
                    alertsWrapper.appendChild(alertDiv);
                });
            } else {
                const cleanMsg = document.createElement('div');
                cleanMsg.className = "alert-item";
                cleanMsg.style.borderLeftColor = "var(--accent-green)";
                cleanMsg.innerHTML = `<p style="color: var(--accent-green); font-weight: bold; margin:0;">[+] Monitoring socket boundaries. No signatures matched on active wire frames.</p>`;
                alertsWrapper.appendChild(cleanMsg);
            }
        } catch (e) {
            console.error("Error connecting to live server telemetry socket:", e);
        }
    }

    async function clearLiveMetrics() {
        clearInterval(livePollingInterval);
        await fetch('/live-sniffer/clear', { method: 'POST' });
        document.getElementById('alerts-wrapper').innerHTML = '';
        document.getElementById('res-alert-count').innerText = '0';
        document.getElementById('analytics-visualization-row').style.display = 'none';
        if (timelineChartInstance) timelineChartInstance.destroy();
        if (severityChartInstance) severityChartInstance.destroy();
        toggleLiveCapture(false);
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // HISTORICAL FILE INGESTION PIPELINE MANAGEMENT
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    document.getElementById('upload-form').addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        
        if (livePollingInterval) toggleLiveCapture(false);

        const fileInput = document.getElementById('file-input');
        const overrideSelect = document.getElementById('override-select');
        const aiCheckbox = document.getElementById('ai-checkbox');
        const submitBtn = document.getElementById('submit-btn');
        const progressContainer = document.getElementById('progress-container');
        const progressFill = document.getElementById('progress-fill');
        const statusMessage = document.getElementById('status-message');
        
        const placeholder = document.getElementById('initial-placeholder');
        const resultsDisplay = document.getElementById('results-display'); // <-- FIXED HERE
        const alertsWrapper = document.getElementById('alerts-wrapper');
        const aiReportWrapper = document.getElementById('ai-report-wrapper');

        if (!fileInput.files.length) return;

        submitBtn.disabled = true;
        placeholder.style.display = 'none';
        resultsDisplay.style.display = 'block';
        alertsWrapper.innerHTML = '';
        aiReportWrapper.style.display = 'none';
        
        progressContainer.style.display = 'block';
        progressFill.style.width = '10%';
        statusMessage.innerText = "Initializing file ingestion pipeline...";

        const formData = new FormData();
        formData.append('file', fileInput.files[0]);
        formData.append('override_type', overrideSelect.value);
        formData.append('run_ai', aiCheckbox.checked);

        let progress = 10;
        const progressInterval = setInterval(() => {
            if (progress < 85) {
                progress += Math.floor(Math.random() * 8) + 3;
                if (progress > 85) progress = 85;
                progressFill.style.width = `${progress}%`;
                
                if (progress < 35) {
                    statusMessage.innerText = "Applying data structure parsing models...";
                } else if (progress < 65) {
                    statusMessage.innerText = "Executing pluggable cross-protocol signature matrices...";
                } else {
                    statusMessage.innerText = aiCheckbox.checked ? 
                        "Local AI model engaged. Evaluating payload indicators (takes a moment)..." : 
                        "Finalizing analytical telemetry data...";
                }
            }
        }, 400);

        try {
            const response = await fetch('/analyze-async', {
                method: 'POST',
                body: formData
            });
            
            clearInterval(progressInterval);
            if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`Pipeline HTTP status breakage: ${response.status}`);

            const data = await response.json();

            progressFill.style.width = '100%';
            statusMessage.innerText = "Analysis matrix completed.";

            document.getElementById('res-filename').innerText = data.filename;
            document.getElementById('res-log-type').innerText = data.log_type;
            document.getElementById('res-alert-count').innerText = data.alerts ? data.alerts.length : 0;

            // Trigger charting sequence for file assets
            renderAnalyticsCharts(data.alerts);

            // 1. BOUNDARY CHECK: Parser Override Failures
            if (data.mismatch_detected && (!data.alerts || data.alerts.length === 0) && (!data.ai_report || data.ai_report.includes("Ingestion stream empty"))) {
                document.getElementById('analytics-visualization-row').style.display = 'none';
                alertsWrapper.innerHTML = `
                    <div style="border: 2px dashed #ff5722; background: rgba(255, 87, 34, 0.1); padding: 20px; border-radius: 6px; margin: 15px 0;">
                        <h4 style="color: #ff5722; margin: 0 0 8px 0; font-size: 1.15em;">❌ Ingestion Blocked: Total Parser Incompatibility</h4>
                        <p style="margin: 4px 0; line-height: 1.5;">
                            You forced execution routing to the <code style="background: #0f1015; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 4px; color: #ff5722;">${data.log_type}</code> engine.<br>
                            Because this file actually contains <code style="background: #0f1015; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 4px; color: #00adb5;">${data.auto_detect_type}</code> syntax, the selected parser could not normalize a single line of data.
                        </p>
                    </div>`;
                aiReportWrapper.style.display = 'none';
            } 
            else {
                // 2. CASE: Manual Playbook Compilation
                if (data.playbook_meta && data.playbook_meta.file_created) {
                    const playbookPanel = document.createElement('div');
                    playbookPanel.style.background = 'var(--bg-primary)';
                    playbookPanel.style.border = '1px dashed var(--accent-cyan)';
                    playbookPanel.style.padding = '15px';
                    playbookPanel.style.borderRadius = '6px';
                    playbookPanel.style.marginBottom = '18px';
                    
                    playbookPanel.innerHTML = `
                        <h4 style="color: var(--accent-cyan); margin: 0 0 8px 0; display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 6px;">
                            📋 On-Demand Remediation Playbook Compiled
                        </h4>
                        <p style="margin: 0 0 10px 0; font-size: 0.9em; color: var(--text-light);">
                            SentinelLite has formulated an explicit security mitigation script file containing <strong>${data.playbook_meta.actionable_targets}</strong> actionable infrastructure targets.
                        </p>
                        <p style="margin: 0; font-size: 0.85em; color: var(--text-muted);">
                            <strong>Local Storage Artifact Path:</strong> <code style="color: var(--accent-cyan); background: var(--bg-dark); padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 4px;">${data.playbook_meta.output_path}</code>
                        </p>
                    `;
                    alertsWrapper.appendChild(playbookPanel);
                }

                // 3. CASE: Standard Warnings
                if (data.mismatch_detected) {
                    const warnDiv = document.createElement('div');
                    warnDiv.style.border = '1px dashed var(--accent-orange)';
                    warnDiv.style.background = 'rgba(255, 87, 34, 0.05)';
                    warnDiv.style.padding = '12px';
                    warnDiv.style.borderRadius = '4px';
                    warnDiv.style.marginBottom = '15px';
                    warnDiv.style.fontSize = '0.9em';
                    warnDiv.innerHTML = `⚠ <strong>Structural Boundary Override Mismatch:</strong> Forced <code>${data.log_type}</code> parser but identified file as <code>${data.auto_detect_type}</code>.`;
                    alertsWrapper.appendChild(warnDiv);
                }

                // Render Signature Alerts
                if (data.alerts && data.alerts.length > 0) {
                    data.alerts.forEach(alert => {
                        const alertDiv = document.createElement('div');
                        alertDiv.className = `alert-item severity-${alert.severity}`;
                        alertDiv.innerHTML = `
                            <h4 style="margin: 0 0 8px 0; font-size: 1.05em;">${alert.title} [${alert.severity}]</h4>
                            <p style="margin: 4px 0; font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Culprit Actor Anchor:</strong> <code>${alert.source}</code></p>
                            <p style="margin: 6px 0 0 0; color: var(--text-muted); font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Risk Rationalization:</strong> ${alert.why_it_matters}</p>
                        `;
                        alertsWrapper.appendChild(alertDiv);
                    });
                } else {
                    alertsWrapper.innerHTML += `
                        <div class="alert-item" style="border-left-color: var(--accent-green); background: rgba(78, 159, 61, 0.05)">
                            <p style="color: var(--accent-green); font-weight: bold; margin: 0; font-size: 0.9em;">
                                [+] Ingestion cycle clean. Context profiles clear of static rule heuristic triggers.
                            </p>
                        </div>`;
                }

                // Append local AI Coprocessor response metrics
                if (aiCheckbox.checked && data.ai_report && !data.ai_report.includes("Ingestion stream empty")) {
                    let formattedText = data.ai_report
                        .replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>')
                        .replace(/^\*\s(.*)$/gm, '<li>$1</li>')
                        .replace(/^\d\.\s(.*)$/gm, '<li>$1</li>')
                        .replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
                    
                    document.getElementById('res-ai-text').innerHTML = formattedText;
                    aiReportWrapper.style.display = 'block';
                }
            }

        } catch (error) {
            clearInterval(progressInterval);
            statusMessage.innerText = "Pipeline process execution crashed.";
            alert(`Execution Error: ${error.message}`);
        } finally {
            submitBtn.disabled = false;
            setTimeout(() => { progressContainer.style.display = 'none'; }, 1000);
        }
    });
</script>

Apply this update, clear your browser cache with Ctrl + F5 (or Cmd + Shift + R), and deploy your telemetry log again. The visualization panels and alerts should render immediately!

is there anything you can think of to improve this project further without vastly widening the scope?

Since you already have a high-performing backend core and a functioning dashboard layout, the best way to elevate this project isn’t by adding massive new features, but by tightening defensive resilience, code quality, and developer experience.

Here are four high-impact, low-scope enhancements that make the project look like a hardened, production-ready security engineering tool.
1. Graceful Multi-Threaded Shutdown Handling

Right now, if you terminate the Flask server using Ctrl+C while the live packet sniffer is active, the background thread can hang in memory or throw ugly socket binding exceptions (OSError: [Errno 98] Address already in use).

You can clean this up with a tiny architectural addition using Python’s native atexit or signal handlers inside app.py.
Python

# Inside app.py
import atexit
from core.live_sniffer import LiveSnifferManager, LIVE_SNIFFER_ACTIVE

def cleanup_background_threads():
    if LIVE_SNIFFER_ACTIVE:
        print("\n[*] System signal caught. Force closing active wire sockets...")
        sniffer = LiveSnifferManager()
        sniffer.stop()

# Registers the callback to fire immediately on server termination
atexit.register(cleanup_background_threads)

2. Frontend Polish: Real-Time Dynamic Chart Streaming

Instead of wiping and redrawing your line chart from scratch every 1.5 seconds during live sniffing, you can push data directly into Chart.js's native array index. This creates a smooth, animated, horizontal moving window just like a real enterprise SOC dashboard.

Update the live stream logic inside renderAnalyticsCharts to append new values seamlessly:
JavaScript

// A low-overhead way to update live timeline charts seamlessly
if (timelineChartInstance && timelineLabels.length > 0) {
    timelineChartInstance.data.labels = timelineLabels;
    timelineChartInstance.data.datasets[0].data = timelineData;
    timelineChartInstance.update('none'); // updates without jagged refresh animations
}

3. Add Robust Exception Isolation to the Parsers

If an attacker introduces a mangled, malformed line inside a log file (or drops a dirty frame on the wire), it shouldn't crash your entire analysis pipeline. Making your parsing methods bulletproof with granular line-by-line exception isolation ensures high availability.

Inside your parser classes (e.g., SyslogParser or WebLogParser), wrap the line iterations like this:
Python

def parse(self, file_path):
    normalized_events = []
    with open(file_path, 'r') as f:
        for line_num, line in enumerate(f, 1):
            try:
                # parsing logic here...
                pass
            except Exception as e:
                # Log the malformed line index but keep processing the rest of the stream
                print(f"[!] Warning: Structural parsing bypass on line {line_num}: {e}")
                continue
    return normalized_events

4. Create an Elegant Technical README.md

The code itself is impressive, but a polished README.md file in your root folder is what sells the project on GitHub or to an engineering manager. It proves you understand system architecture and deployment pipelines.

Structure it with clean, skimmable headers:

    Architecture Diagram: A simple text-based ASCII flow map showing how raw input logs/network sockets bypass anomalies, feed into the correlation rule manager, step through the SOAR matrix, and hit the UI canvas.

    Prerequisites: Note your key dependencies (Flask, Scapy, Ollama/Requests).

    Deployment Instructions: Give clear commands for installing scapy (pip install scapy) and running the app.

    Security Notice: Mention that capturing raw telemetry matrices requires local administrative permissions (e.g., running with sudo on Linux or an administrative shell on Windows to bind to network interfaces).

Implementing these updates wraps your existing logic in production-grade error boundaries and makes the entire system incredibly robust.

Are you looking to tie up these loose ends on the server, or would you like to start building out that tailored technical resume layout to showcase this framework?

hmmm, I think the project seemed cleanest and most direct before the last two updates we made (the dashboard with graphs and the live capture). lets remove those from the frontend

I completely respect that instinct. In software engineering—especially security tools—less is often much more. Stripping out the background networking threads and heavy charting libraries returns the framework to a lean, hyper-focused, lightning-fast log analysis utility.

It eliminates client-side polling overhead, drops external CDN dependencies, and keeps the code incredibly readable.

<script>
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // HISTORICAL FILE INGESTION PIPELINE MANAGEMENT
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    document.getElementById('upload-form').addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        const fileInput = document.getElementById('file-input');
        const overrideSelect = document.getElementById('override-select');
        const aiCheckbox = document.getElementById('ai-checkbox');
        const submitBtn = document.getElementById('submit-btn');
        const progressContainer = document.getElementById('progress-container');
        const progressFill = document.getElementById('progress-fill');
        const statusMessage = document.getElementById('status-message');
        
        const placeholder = document.getElementById('initial-placeholder');
        const resultsDisplay = document.getElementById('results-display');
        const alertsWrapper = document.getElementById('alerts-wrapper');
        const aiReportWrapper = document.getElementById('ai-report-wrapper');

        if (!fileInput.files.length) return;

        // UI Lockdown State
        submitBtn.disabled = true;
        placeholder.style.display = 'none';
        resultsDisplay.style.display = 'block';
        alertsWrapper.innerHTML = '';
        aiReportWrapper.style.display = 'none';
        
        progressContainer.style.display = 'block';
        progressFill.style.width = '10%';
        statusMessage.innerText = "Initializing file ingestion pipeline...";

        const formData = new FormData();
        formData.append('file', fileInput.files[0]);
        formData.append('override_type', overrideSelect.value);
        formData.append('run_ai', aiCheckbox.checked);

        // Progress Ticker Loop Simulation
        let progress = 10;
        const progressInterval = setInterval(() => {
            if (progress < 85) {
                progress += Math.floor(Math.random() * 8) + 3;
                if (progress > 85) progress = 85;
                progressFill.style.width = `${progress}%`;
                
                if (progress < 35) {
                    statusMessage.innerText = "Applying data structure parsing models...";
                } else if (progress < 65) {
                    statusMessage.innerText = "Executing pluggable cross-protocol signature matrices...";
                } else {
                    statusMessage.innerText = aiCheckbox.checked ? 
                        "Local AI model engaged. Evaluating payload indicators (takes a moment)..." : 
                        "Finalizing analytical telemetry data...";
                }
            }
        }, 400);

        try {
            const response = await fetch('/analyze-async', {
                method: 'POST',
                body: formData
            });
            
            clearInterval(progressInterval);
            if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`Pipeline HTTP status breakage: ${response.status}`);

            const data = await response.json();

            progressFill.style.width = '100%';
            statusMessage.innerText = "Analysis matrix completed.";

            document.getElementById('res-filename').innerText = data.filename;
            document.getElementById('res-log-type').innerText = data.log_type;
            document.getElementById('res-alert-count').innerText = data.alerts ? data.alerts.length : 0;

            // 1. BOUNDARY CHECK: Parser Override Failures
            if (data.mismatch_detected && (!data.alerts || data.alerts.length === 0) && (!data.ai_report || data.ai_report.includes("Ingestion stream empty"))) {
                alertsWrapper.innerHTML = `
                    <div style="border: 2px dashed #ff5722; background: rgba(255, 87, 34, 0.1); padding: 20px; border-radius: 6px; margin: 15px 0;">
                        <h4 style="color: #ff5722; margin: 0 0 8px 0; font-size: 1.15em;">❌ Ingestion Blocked: Total Parser Incompatibility</h4>
                        <p style="margin: 4px 0; line-height: 1.5;">
                            You forced execution routing to the <code style="background: #0f1015; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 4px; color: #ff5722;">${data.log_type}</code> engine.<br>
                            Because this file actually contains <code style="background: #0f1015; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 4px; color: #00adb5;">${data.auto_detect_type}</code> syntax, the selected parser could not normalize a single line of data.
                        </p>
                    </div>`;
                aiReportWrapper.style.display = 'none';
            } 
            else {
                // 2. CASE: Manual Playbook Compilation
                if (data.playbook_meta && data.playbook_meta.file_created) {
                    const playbookPanel = document.createElement('div');
                    playbookPanel.style.background = 'var(--bg-primary)';
                    playbookPanel.style.border = '1px dashed var(--accent-cyan)';
                    playbookPanel.style.padding = '15px';
                    playbookPanel.style.borderRadius = '6px';
                    playbookPanel.style.marginBottom = '18px';
                    
                    playbookPanel.innerHTML = `
                        <h4 style="color: var(--accent-cyan); margin: 0 0 8px 0; display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 6px;">
                            📋 On-Demand Remediation Playbook Compiled
                        </h4>
                        <p style="margin: 0 0 10px 0; font-size: 0.9em; color: var(--text-light);">
                            SentinelLite has formulated an explicit security mitigation script file containing <strong>${data.playbook_meta.actionable_targets}</strong> actionable infrastructure targets.
                        </p>
                        <p style="margin: 0; font-size: 0.85em; color: var(--text-muted);">
                            <strong>Local Storage Artifact Path:</strong> <code style="color: var(--accent-cyan); background: var(--bg-dark); padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 4px;">${data.playbook_meta.output_path}</code>
                        </p>
                    `;
                    alertsWrapper.appendChild(playbookPanel);
                }

                // 3. CASE: Standard Warnings
                if (data.mismatch_detected) {
                    const warnDiv = document.createElement('div');
                    warnDiv.style.border = '1px dashed var(--accent-orange)';
                    warnDiv.style.background = 'rgba(255, 87, 34, 0.05)';
                    warnDiv.style.padding = '12px';
                    warnDiv.style.borderRadius = '4px';
                    warnDiv.style.marginBottom = '15px';
                    warnDiv.style.fontSize = '0.9em';
                    warnDiv.innerHTML = `⚠ <strong>Structural Boundary Override Mismatch:</strong> Forced <code>${data.log_type}</code> parser but identified file as <code>${data.auto_detect_type}</code>.`;
                    alertsWrapper.appendChild(warnDiv);
                }

                // Render Signature Alerts
                if (data.alerts && data.alerts.length > 0) {
                    data.alerts.forEach(alert => {
                        const alertDiv = document.createElement('div');
                        alertDiv.className = `alert-item severity-${alert.severity}`;
                        alertDiv.innerHTML = `
                            <h4 style="margin: 0 0 8px 0; font-size: 1.05em;">${alert.title} [${alert.severity}]</h4>
                            <p style="margin: 4px 0; font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Culprit Actor Anchor:</strong> <code>${alert.source}</code></p>
                            <p style="margin: 6px 0 0 0; color: var(--text-muted); font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Risk Rationalization:</strong> ${alert.why_it_matters}</p>
                        `;
                        alertsWrapper.appendChild(alertDiv);
                    });
                } else {
                    alertsWrapper.innerHTML += `
                        <div class="alert-item" style="border-left-color: var(--accent-green); background: rgba(78, 159, 61, 0.05)">
                            <p style="color: var(--accent-green); font-weight: bold; margin: 0; font-size: 0.9em;">
                                [+] Ingestion cycle clean. Context profiles clear of static rule heuristic triggers.
                            </p>
                        </div>`;
                }

                // Append local AI Coprocessor response metrics
                if (aiCheckbox.checked && data.ai_report && !data.ai_report.includes("Ingestion stream empty")) {
                    let formattedText = data.ai_report
                        .replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>')
                        .replace(/^\*\s(.*)$/gm, '<li>$1</li>')
                        .replace(/^\d\.\s(.*)$/gm, '<li>$1</li>')
                        .replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
                    
                    document.getElementById('res-ai-text').innerHTML = formattedText;
                    aiReportWrapper.style.display = 'block';
                }
            }

        } catch (error) {
            clearInterval(progressInterval);
            statusMessage.innerText = "Pipeline process execution crashed.";
            alert(`Execution Error: ${error.message}`);
        } finally {
            submitBtn.disabled = false;
            setTimeout(() => { progressContainer.style.display = 'none'; }, 1000);
        }
    });
</script>
</body>
</html>

The application is now back to its clean, functional baseline. You can safely delete core/live_sniffer.py if you'd like to completely purge the unused backend code as well.
