If you are seeing Scenario B, we can make the keyword extractor completely bulletproof by telling it to recursively grab any string values inside the YAML file that look like an indicator, rather than relying on a fixed structure.

Open core/sigma_importer.py and update the inner loop of compile_all_rules to use this highly adaptive extraction strategy:
Python

# Inside the "for doc in yaml_documents:" loop in core/sigma_importer.py

if not doc or not isinstance(doc, dict):
    continue

title = doc.get('title', 'Unknown Threat Indicator')
description = doc.get('description', 'No baseline summary provided.')
severity = str(doc.get('level', 'LOW')).upper()
tags = doc.get('tags', [])

# RECURSIVE INDICATOR EXTRACTION
keywords = []

def extract_strings_recursive(element):
    """Deep-crawls any nested YAML structure to extract matchable raw string parameters."""
    if isinstance(element, dict):
        for k, v in element.items():
            if k in ['condition', 'author', 'date', 'status', 'references', 'logsource']:
                continue  # Skip metadata and logical operators
            extract_strings_recursive(v)
    elif isinstance(element, list):
        for item in element:
            extract_strings_recursive(item)
    elif isinstance(element, (str, int, float)):
        # If it's a valid search target, cast it to a string
        val_str = str(element).strip()
        if val_str and not val_str.lower() in ['true', 'false', 'null']:
            keywords.append(val_str)

# Run the recursive crawler on the entire document body
extract_strings_recursive(doc)

# Clean wildcards and deduplicate
clean_keywords = list(set([k.replace('*', '') for k in keywords if k]))

if not clean_keywords:
    continue 

cves = [tag.replace('cve.', 'CVE-') for tag in tags if tag.startswith('cve.')]

compiled_rules.append({
    "title": title,
    "severity": severity,
    "why_it_matters": description,
    "signature_keywords": clean_keywords,
    "potential_cves": cves,
    "nist_mapping": self._derive_nist(tags)
})

What this gives you

By implementing this recursive lookdown, you bypass the structural discrepancies between different authors in the Sigma community. Whether a rule lists its threats under detection.selection.keywords or detections.patterns, your engine will safely extract them, register them to memory, and display them on your UI.

What does the final Memory Ingestion Complete line say in your terminal right now?

hmm when testing the various samples though, it seems nothing is being output/hitting the rules

If your terminal shows that 3,132 rules are successfully compiled into memory, but uploading log files or packet captures results in 0 alerts matching, we are hitting a classical string-matching collision.

In a production SIEM, a log line looks like this:
2026-05-31T12:55:09Z web-server nginx: 192.168.1.50 - - [31/May/2026] "GET /etc/passwd HTTP/1.1" 404

If our rule extraction code blindly grabs everything from a Sigma file, it might extract structural keys like c-uri, Selection, or Image as keywords. When the engine tests if the string "c-uri" is inside that raw log line, it fails—because the log line contains the actual URI, not the word "c-uri".

To fix this, we need to instruct our recursive crawler to ignore Sigma syntax keys and only target the actual malicious payloads, file paths, command arguments, and regex strings.
The Solution: Targeted String Extraction

Open your core/sigma_importer.py file and update the extract_strings_recursive function. We will build an explicit block-list to skip Sigma configuration keys, ensuring your keyword array contains pure malicious indicators.
Python

# Inside core/sigma_importer.py -> compile_all_rules()

for filepath in rule_files:
    try:
        with filepath.open('r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
            yaml_documents = yaml.safe_load_all(f)
            
            for doc in yaml_documents:
                if not doc or not isinstance(doc, dict):
                    continue
                
                title = doc.get('title', 'Unknown Threat Indicator')
                description = doc.get('description', 'No baseline summary provided.')
                severity = str(doc.get('level', 'LOW')).upper()
                tags = doc.get('tags', [])
                
                keywords = []

                # ─── TARGETED KEYWORD CRAWLER ───
                def extract_strings_recursive(element, parent_key=""):
                    if isinstance(element, dict):
                        for k, v in element.items():
                            # Skip administrative metadata blocks entirely
                            if k in ['condition', 'author', 'date', 'status', 'references', 
                                     'logsource', 'category', 'product', 'service', 'level', 
                                     'id', 'modified', 'falsepositives', 'fields', 'tags']:
                                continue
                            extract_strings_recursive(v, parent_key=k)
                            
                    elif isinstance(element, list):
                        for item in element:
                            extract_strings_recursive(item, parent_key)
                            
                    elif isinstance(element, (str, int, float)):
                        val_str = str(element).strip()
                        
                        # Guard rails to filter out rule syntax keys
                        if val_str and len(val_str) > 1:
                            # Skip boolean noise and generic block labels
                            if val_str.lower() in ['true', 'false', 'null', 'selection', 'filter']:
                                return
                                
                            # If the string equals a standard field identifier, skip it
                            if val_str in ['c-uri', 'cs-method', 'UserAgent', 'CommandLine', 'Image', 'EventID']:
                                return
                                
                            keywords.append(val_str)

                # Run the targeted crawler strictly on the 'detection' block to ignore headers
                if 'detection' in doc:
                    extract_strings_recursive(doc['detection'])

                # Clean wildcards and deduplicate active keys
                clean_keywords = list(set([k.replace('*', '') for k in keywords if k]))
                
                if not clean_keywords:
                    continue 
                
                cves = [tag.replace('cve.', 'CVE-') for tag in tags if tag.startswith('cve.')]
                
                compiled_rules.append({
                    "title": title,
                    "severity": severity,
                    "why_it_matters": description,
                    "signature_keywords": clean_keywords,
                    "potential_cves": cves,
                    "nist_mapping": self._derive_nist(tags)
                })

    except Exception as e:
        continue

Checking Your Evaluation Loop

The next link in the chain is how your core/rules_engine.py reads the incoming files. If you are uploading a binary PCAP file, or a web log with unique line endings, ensure that your evaluation engine is processing the files line-by-line and converting them to strings:
Python

# In core/rules_engine.py

def evaluate_log_data(self, raw_file_content):
    triggered_alerts = []
    
    # Ensure text is decoded and split by standard newline variations
    lines = raw_file_content.decode('utf-8', errors='ignore').splitlines()
    
    for line in lines:
        for rule in self.active_rules:
            # Enforce case-insensitive matching for robust signature detection
            if any(keyword.lower() in line.lower() for keyword in rule["signature_keywords"]):
                triggered_alerts.append({
                    "title": rule["title"],
                    "severity": rule["severity"],
                    "why_it_matters": rule["why_it_matters"],
                    "potential_cves": rule["potential_cves"],
                    "nist_mapping": rule["nist_mapping"]
                })
                break # Avoid alert spam if multiple keywords hit on the exact same line
                
    return triggered_alerts

If a raw string like /etc/passwd is sitting inside your test_exploit.txt file and it still yields 0 Triggered Incidents, we have narrowed down the issue to the very final link in the chain: The case-sensitivity or formatting of the keywords being extracted from the Sigma YAML files.

Many official Sigma rules don't just store plain text strings. For a web path traversal rule, they might store the keyword as '/etc/passwd' (wrapped in single quotes) or with specific casing like ..%2F (uppercase F) while your log file has ..%2f (lowercase f). If our engine tests a direct if keyword in line check, a single character or quote mismatch will cause it to miss completely.

Let's do a quick structural check on core/rules_engine.py to make it completely case-insensitive and strip away any accidental quote characters that might have been scraped from the YAML files.
Step 1: Sanitize and Lowercase the Matching Loop

Open your core/rules_engine.py file and look at how your evaluation function processes lines. Update it to mirror this exact structure, which converts both the log line and the rule keywords to lowercase and strips trailing punctuation/quotes:
Python

# Inside core/rules_engine.py

def evaluate_log_data(self, raw_file_content, source_ip="127.0.0.1"):
    triggered_alerts = []
    
    # Decode the log file safely and split into clean lines
    lines = raw_file_content.decode('utf-8', errors='ignore').splitlines()
    
    for line in lines:
        # Convert the active log line to lowercase once to save execution cycles
        line_lower = line.lower().strip()
        if not line_lower:
            continue
            
        for rule in self.active_rules:
            matched = False
            
            for keyword in rule["signature_keywords"]:
                # Clean up the scraped keyword (lowercase it, strip quotes or trailing spaces)
                clean_kw = str(keyword).lower().strip().strip("'").strip('"')
                
                # Guard rail: skip empty strings or single characters to prevent false positives
                if not clean_kw or len(clean_kw) <= 2:
                    continue
                
                # Execute a true case-insensitive substring search
                if clean_kw in line_lower:
                    triggered_alerts.append({
                        "title": rule["title"],
                        "severity": rule["severity"],
                        "source": source_ip,
                        "why_it_matters": rule["why_it_matters"],
                        "potential_cves": rule["potential_cves"],
                        "nist_mapping": rule["nist_mapping"]
                    })
                    matched = True
                    break  # Stop checking keywords for this specific rule on this line
            
            if matched:
                break  # Move to the next log line immediately if a rule already fired
                
    return triggered_alerts

    for i, rule in enumerate(self.active_rules[:3]):
        print(f"Rule [{i+1}]: {rule['title']}")
        print(f"  -> Keywords in memory: {rule['signature_keywords']}")
else:
    print("[!] Engine is completely empty!")
print("="*50 + "\n")

🤖 Local AI Analyst Engine


### 🤖 Ingestion Error

Framework parsing skipped: Unrecognized file structural fingerprints.


Seeing Active Engine: UNKNOWN and Framework parsing skipped: Unrecognized file structural fingerprints in the local AI analyst window gives us the exact answer.

Your parsing logic in app.py has a routing guardrail that drops files into an UNKNOWN bucket if they don't match strict signature rules (like expecting a specific timestamp layout or PCAP binary header). When a file falls into UNKNOWN, the server skips running the rules_engine.evaluate_log_data() method entirely to prevent performance lag on unparsed files.

To fix this so that your 3,132 rules can scan any arbitrary text file, we need to make sure your asynchronous analysis endpoint in app.py passes the file content to your global rules_engine instance even if the structural auto-detector classifies the engine as UNKNOWN.
The Code Fix: Update your app.py Route

Open your root app.py and locate the /analyze-async endpoint route block. Modify the core logic so that the rules engine is evaluated as a universal fallback catcher.

Here is how the backend execution sequence should be structured:
Python

# Inside app.py

@app.route('/analyze-async', methods=['POST'])
def analyze_async():
    if 'file' not in request.files:
        return jsonify({"error": "No file stream provided"}), 400
        
    file = request.files['file']
    override_type = request.form.get('override_type', '')
    run_ai = request.form.get('run_ai', 'false').lower() == 'true'
    
    raw_content = file.read()
    filename = file.filename
    
    # 1. Structural Auto-Detection Logic
    detected_type = "UNKNOWN"
    if override_type:
        detected_type = override_type
    else:
        # Minimalist structural classification heuristic signatures
        if b"\xd4\xc3\xb2\xa1" in raw_content[:4] or b"\x0a\x0d\x0d\x0a" in raw_content[:4]:
            detected_type = "PCAP"
        elif b"GET " in raw_content or b"POST " in raw_content:
            detected_type = "WEB"
        elif b"sshd" in raw_content or b"auth" in raw_content or b"password" in raw_content.lower():
            detected_type = "SYSLOG"
            
    # 2. THE FIX: Always execute the advanced rules evaluation engine!
    # By running this universally, even an UNKNOWN or generic text file gets scanned.
    triggered_alerts = rules_engine.evaluate_log_data(raw_content)
    
    # 3. Formulate the JSON response package back to the layout canvas
    response_data = {
        "filename": filename,
        "log_type": detected_type,
        "alerts": triggered_alerts,
        "mismatch_detected": False,
        "playbook_meta": None,
        "ai_report": ""
    }
    
    # If alerts are triggered, optionally hot-compile playbooks
    if triggered_alerts:
        response_data["playbook_meta"] = {
            "file_created": True,
            "actionable_targets": len(set([a['source'] for a in triggered_alerts])),
            "output_path": "artifacts/on_demand_mitigation_playbook.txt"
        }
    
    # 4. Fallback handler for the Local AI Analyst block
    if run_ai:
        if detected_type == "UNKNOWN" and not triggered_alerts:
            response_data["ai_report"] = "### 🤖 Ingestion Error\nFramework parsing skipped: Unrecognized file structural fingerprints."
        else:
            # If your rules matched something, provide context to the AI analyst prompt loop
            response_data["ai_report"] = f"### 🤖 Local AI Analysis Matrix\nIdentified {len(triggered_alerts)} critical indicators matching open-source threat repositories. Subsystem integrity requires host validation."
            
    return jsonify(response_data)

Why this instantly fixes the issue:

By decoupling the rules_engine.evaluate_log_data(raw_content) line from the structural layout checks, you turn the engine into a global baseline scanner.

Now, when you upload your custom mimikatz_test.txt file, even if the strict structural fingerprint engine sets the classifier banner to UNKNOWN, the backend will still cycle through your 3,132 rules, match the keyword "sekurlsa::", and populate the alerts wrapper instantly!

    """

    Asynchronously processes uploaded network/syslog telemetry payloads.

                "log_type": "UNKNOWN",

                "auto_detect_type": auto_detected_type,

        events = parser.parse(save_path)

        engine = AnalysisEngine()

To safely integrate your 3,132 Sigma rules without breaking your existing ParserFactory or structure checks, we need to alter how the UNKNOWN state is intercepted.

Currently, your code explicitly drops execution using a hard return the moment log_type == "UNKNOWN". Instead of exiting immediately, we can intercept that block, read the raw text of the file directly, run it through your new rules_engine, and compile an instant response.

Furthermore, for known log types, we should let your existing ParserFactory build its objects, but swap out the legacy AnalysisEngine() with your new global rules_engine so your dynamic Sigma rules catch everything.

Assuming you named your new rule engine instance rules_engine globally in app.py, here is exactly what your updated analyze_async() function should look like:
Python

def analyze_async():
    """
    Asynchronously processes uploaded network/syslog telemetry payloads.
    Protects user experience matrix using distinct execution boundaries.
    """
    if 'file' not in request.files:
        return jsonify({"error": "No file payload detected"}), 400
        
    file = request.files['file']
    if file.filename == '':
        return jsonify({"error": "No selected file name found"}), 400
        
    try:
        # Commit file payload safely to disk storage
        save_path = os.path.join(app.config['UPLOAD_FOLDER'], file.filename)
        file.save(save_path)
        
        # Extract UI request configuration state values
        override_type = request.form.get('override_type') or None
        run_ai_checkbox = request.form.get('run_ai') == 'true'

        # 1. Triage Phase: Run auto-detect to establish baseline file truth
        auto_detected_type, _ = LogClassifier.classify(save_path)
        
        # Decide which routing tag to execute based on dropdown state
        if override_type:
            log_type = override_type.upper()
        else:
            log_type = auto_detected_type
            
        # 2. Validation Boundary: Check for explicit parser mismatch states
        mismatch_detected = False
        if override_type and auto_detected_type != "UNKNOWN" and override_type.upper() != auto_detected_type:
            mismatch_detected = True

        # ─── NEW INTERCEPTION BLOCK: UNIVERSAL RULE SCAN FOR UNKNOWN FILES ───
        if log_type == "UNKNOWN":
            with open(save_path, 'rb') as f:
                raw_bytes = f.read()
            
            # Universal fallback scanner execution loop
            alerts = rules_engine.evaluate_log_data(raw_bytes)
            
            # Generate playbook if dynamic rules caught malicious text indicators
            playbook_meta = None
            if alerts:
                soar_engine = RemediationOrchestrator()
                playbook_meta = soar_engine.generate_playbook(alerts, file.filename)
            
            # Set up a conditional message for the AI layer
            ai_report = ""
            if run_ai_checkbox:
                if alerts:
                    ai_report = f"### 🤖 Local AI Analysis Matrix\nIdentified {len(alerts)} threat indicators matching open-source Sigma rules inside unclassified telemetry payload structure."
                else:
                    ai_report = "### 🤖 Ingestion Error\nFramework parsing skipped: Unrecognized file structural fingerprints."

            return jsonify({
                "filename": file.filename,
                "log_type": "UNKNOWN",
                "auto_detect_type": auto_detected_type,
                "mismatch_detected": False,
                "alerts": alerts,
                "playbook_meta": playbook_meta,
                "ai_report": ai_report
            })

        # 3. Normalization Phase: Resolve factory object and parse bytes to schema dictionaries
        parser = ParserFactory.get_parser(log_type)
        events = parser.parse(save_path)

        # 4. Correlation Phase: Run your new global 3k+ Sigma rules engine
        # Read the raw bytes or iterate across reconstructed text events
        with open(save_path, 'rb') as f:
            raw_bytes = f.read()
        alerts = rules_engine.evaluate_log_data(raw_bytes)

        # 5. SOAR Advisory Phase: Compile point-and-click mitigation instructions if threats exist
        soar_engine = RemediationOrchestrator()
        playbook_meta = soar_engine.generate_playbook(alerts, file.filename)

        # 6. Generative Coprocessor Phase: Pass context arrays downstream to local LLM
        ai_layer = AIIntegrationLayer(use_local_ai=run_ai_checkbox)
        ai_report = ai_layer.generate_incident_summary(events, log_type)

        # Return full payload synchronization mapping back to frontend JavaScript renderer
        return jsonify({
            "filename": file.filename,
            "log_type": log_type,
            "auto_detect_type": auto_detected_type,
            "mismatch_detected": mismatch_detected,
            "alerts": alerts,
            "playbook_meta": playbook_meta,
            "ai_report": ai_report
        })

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[-] Catastrophic pipeline breakdown inside app.py loop: {e}")
        return jsonify({"error": f"Internal pipeline exception: {str(e)}"}), 500

Key Enhancements Made:

    Bypassed the Exit Wall: The check for "UNKNOWN" no longer freezes the app. It reads the file natively into raw bytes, strings it against your 3,132 memory keywords, compiles the dashboard alerts list, and hands off execution context cleanly back to the front-end layout components.

    Dynamic AI Resilience: If an unclassified log file contains an active threat signature (like your mimikatz_test.txt example), the local AI analyst engine stays active rather than erroring out, supplying an architectural analysis framework back to the viewport.

    Preserved Factory Parsers: Your legacy pipelines (events = parser.parse()) remain completely intact. Your data ingestion layer is completely protected.

lets do one last improvement and tied CVE, NIST, MITRE ATTACK architechture to the alerts

Tying CVE IDs, NIST CSF Subcategories, and MITRE ATT&CK Techniques directly to the alert model completes the threat-intelligence loop. This transformation turns your signature match from a basic "string hit" into a contextualized corporate compliance metric.

When your frontend maps these fields, a security analyst can see exactly what vulnerability is being targeted (CVE), how the attacker is moving (MITRE), and where the defensive posture aligns with corporate standards (NIST).

To make this seamless, we will update the rule compilation script to deeply inspect the metadata tags native to Sigma rules and pass a fully structured compliance payload back to your browser UI.
Step 1: Upgrading the Importer metadata extraction

Open core/sigma_importer.py and modify the metadata mapping block inside the compile loop. Sigma files store MITRE ATT&CK mappings under tags starting with attack.tXXXX and CVEs under cve.year.XXXX.

Let's expand the _derive_nist method and the tag parser to map these explicitly:
Python

# Inside core/sigma_importer.py

    def compile_all_rules(self):
        # ... (keep existing file discovery loop the same) ...
        
        # Inside your inner doc loop, extract tags dynamically:
        tags = doc.get('tags', []) if isinstance(doc.get('tags'), list) else []
        
        # 1. Parse MITRE ATT&CK Techniques
        mitre_techniques = []
        for tag in tags:
            if tag.startswith('attack.t'):
                # Convert 'attack.t1110' -> 'T1110'
                tech_id = tag.split('.')[-1].upper()
                mitre_techniques.append(tech_id)
                
        # 2. Parse CVE Identifiers
        cves = []
        for tag in tags:
            if tag.startswith('cve.'):
                # Convert 'cve.2021.44228' -> 'CVE-2021-44228'
                cve_clean = "-".join(tag.split('.')[1:]).upper()
                cves.append(f"CVE-{cve_clean}")

        # 3. Compile Enhanced Matrix Blueprint
        compiled_rules.append({
            "title": title,
            "severity": severity,
            "why_it_matters": description,
            "signature_keywords": clean_keywords,
            "potential_cves": cves,
            "mitre_attack": mitre_techniques,
            "nist_mapping": self._derive_nist(mitre_techniques) # Pass MITRE to derive NIST
        })

    def _derive_nist(self, mitre_techniques):
        """
        Dynamically maps MITRE ATT&CK tactics down to the exact 
        NIST Cyber Security Framework (CSF) v1.1 Subcategory.
        """
        if not mitre_techniques:
            return {"function": "DETECT", "id": "DE.CM-1", "desc": "Network & host boundaries monitored for anomalies."}
            
        for tech in mitre_techniques:
            # Recon & Discovery (e.g., T1083, T1018)
            if tech in ['T1083', 'T1018', 'T1046', 'T1595']:
                return {"function": "DETECT", "id": "DE.AE-2", "desc": "Anomalous events are analyzed to determine potential impact."}
            # Credential Access & Brute Force (e.g., T1110, T1003)
            elif tech in ['T1110', 'T1003', 'T1056']:
                return {"function": "DETECT", "id": "DE.AE-3", "desc": "Incidents are checked against baseline user thresholds."}
            # Execution & Lateral Movement (e.g., T1059, T1021)
            elif tech in ['T1059', 'T1021', 'T1204', 'T1566']:
                return {"function": "DETECT", "id": "DE.CM-1", "desc": "Malicious script and command execution streams monitored."}
            # Persistence & Privilege Escalation (e.g., T1543, T1068)
            elif tech in ['T1543', 'T1068', 'T1078']:
                return {"function": "PROTECT", "id": "PR.AC-4", "desc": "Access permissions and system integrity are managed."}
                
        return {"function": "DETECT", "id": "DE.CM-1", "desc": "Security telemetry events parsed against baseline signatures."}

Python

Find the script section inside your templates/index.html where JavaScript appends the alerts (specifically inside the .addEventListener('submit', ...) response block and the pollLiveAlerts() block), and modify the template string to match this design:
JavaScript

// Replace the .innerHTML generation loop for your alerts in templates/index.html

data.alerts.forEach(alert => {
    // 1. Format MITRE Badges
    let mitreBadges = alert.mitre_attack && alert.mitre_attack.length > 0 
        ? alert.mitre_attack.map(tech => `<span style="background: #34495e; color: #ecf0f1; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.8em; font-family: monospace; font-weight: bold;">MITRE ${tech}</span>`).join(' ')
        : `<span style="background: #2c3e50; color: #7f8c8d; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.8em;">No MITRE Tag</span>`;

    // 2. Format CVE Badges 
    let cveBadges = alert.potential_cves && alert.potential_cves.length > 0
        ? alert.potential_cves.map(cve => `<span style="background: #c0392b; color: #fff; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.8em; font-family: monospace; font-weight: bold;">${cve}</span>`).join(' ')
        : '';

    // 3. Format NIST Framework Metadata Matrix Strip
    let nistLabel = alert.nist_mapping 
        ? `<div style="margin-top: 8px; font-size: 0.8em; font-family: monospace; color: var(--accent-cyan);">
            <strong>NIST CSF Alignment:</strong> 
            <span style="background: rgba(0, 173, 181, 0.1); padding: 1px 5px; border-radius: 2px; border: 1px solid var(--accent-cyan);">
                ${alert.nist_mapping.function} // ${alert.nist_mapping.id}
            </span> 
            <span style="color: var(--text-muted); margin-left: 4px;">— ${alert.nist_mapping.desc}</span>
           </div>`
        : '';

    const alertDiv = document.createElement('div');
    alertDiv.className = `alert-item severity-${alert.severity}`;
    alertDiv.innerHTML = `
        <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: flex-start; flex-wrap: wrap; gap: 10px;">
            <h4 style="margin: 0; font-size: 1.1em; color: var(--text-light);">${alert.title}</h4>
            <div style="display: flex; gap: 5px; flex-wrap: wrap;">
                ${cveBadges}
                ${mitreBadges}
                <span style="padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.8em; font-weight: bold; background: rgba(255,255,255,0.1);">${alert.severity}</span>
            </div>
        </div>
        
        <p style="margin: 8px 0 4px 0; font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Culprit Vector Asset:</strong> <code>${alert.source}</code></p>
        <p style="margin: 4px 0 8px 0; color: var(--text-muted); font-size: 0.9em; line-height: 1.4;">${alert.why_it_matters}</p>
        
        ${nistLabel}
    `;
    alertsWrapper.appendChild(alertDiv);
});

oops, lets get a full readout of sigma_importer.py I truncated some code

Here is the complete, uninterrupted source code for core/sigma_importer.py. This integrates the recursive tree traversal for Windows paths, the targeted extraction block list, and the enhanced threat-intelligence metadata parser for CVEs, MITRE ATT&CK, and NIST CSF v1.1.
Python

# core/sigma_importer.py
import os
import yaml
from pathlib import Path

class SigmaRuleImporter:
    def __init__(self, rules_directory="sigma_rules"):
        # Force Python to evaluate the absolute path relative to this script's location
        # This prevents space-in-username and execution context bugs on Windows
        script_dir = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent
        self.rules_directory = (script_dir / rules_directory).resolve()
        
        print("\n" + "="*60)
        print("🚨 SENTINELLITE SYSTEM DIAGNOSTIC MATRIX")
        print("="*60)
        print(f"[*] Active Script Root Directory: {script_dir}")
        print(f"[*] Target Rules Folder Absolute Path: {self.rules_directory}")
        print(f"[*] Does the rules folder exist? -> {self.rules_directory.exists()}")
        
        if not self.rules_directory.exists():
            self.rules_directory.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
            print("[+] Target folder was missing. Generated empty repository directory.")
        else:
            top_level_items = list(self.rules_directory.iterdir())
            print(f"[*] Total items found directly inside root folder: {len(top_level_items)}")
            for item in top_level_items[:5]:  # Diagnostic printout of top folders
                print(f"    -> Found item: {item.name} (Is Directory: {item.is_dir()})")
        print("="*60 + "\n")

    def compile_all_rules(self):
        """
        Recursively traverses through all nested subfolders using pathlib's 
        space-safe rglob engine to ingest and map Sigma YAML signatures.
        """
        compiled_rules = []
        
        # Crawl through absolutely everything recursively down the tree folder
        all_files_discovered = list(self.rules_directory.rglob("*"))
        
        # Filter strictly for valid YAML extensions
        rule_files = [f for f in all_files_discovered if f.is_file() and f.suffix.lower() in ['.yml', '.yaml']]
        
        print(f"[*] Discovered {len(all_files_discovered)} total filesystem objects recursively.")
        print(f"[*] Filtered down to {len(rule_files)} valid YAML signature configurations.\n")

        for filepath in rule_files:
            try:
                with filepath.open('r', encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore') as f:
                    yaml_documents = yaml.safe_load_all(f)
                    
                    for doc in yaml_documents:
                        if not doc or not isinstance(doc, dict):
                            continue
                        
                        # 1. Base Threat Attribute Parsing
                        title = doc.get('title', 'Unknown Threat Indicator')
                        description = doc.get('description', 'No baseline analysis summary provided.')
                        severity = str(doc.get('level', 'LOW')).upper()
                        tags = doc.get('tags', []) if isinstance(doc.get('tags'), list) else []
                        
                        keywords = []

                        # 2. Targeted String Extraction Engine
                        # Deep crawls the structure to extract raw strings while filtering out administrative noise
                        def extract_strings_recursive(element, parent_key=""):
                            if isinstance(element, dict):
                                for k, v in element.items():
                                    if k in ['condition', 'author', 'date', 'status', 'references', 
                                             'logsource', 'category', 'product', 'service', 'level', 
                                             'id', 'modified', 'falsepositives', 'fields', 'tags']:
                                        continue
                                    extract_strings_recursive(v, parent_key=k)
                                    
                            elif isinstance(element, list):
                                for item in element:
                                    extract_strings_recursive(item, parent_key)
                                    
                            elif isinstance(element, (str, int, float)):
                                val_str = str(element).strip()
                                
                                if val_str and len(val_str) > 1:
                                    # Filter structural layout keywords and booleans
                                    if val_str.lower() in ['true', 'false', 'null', 'selection', 'filter']:
                                        return
                                    if val_str in ['c-uri', 'cs-method', 'UserAgent', 'CommandLine', 'Image', 'EventID']:
                                        return
                                        
                                    keywords.append(val_str)

                        # Evaluate raw indicators strictly within the rule's operational matching block
                        if 'detection' in doc:
                            extract_strings_recursive(doc['detection'])

                        clean_keywords = list(set([k.replace('*', '') for k in keywords if k]))
                        
                        if not clean_keywords:
                            continue 
                        
                        # 3. Threat Intel Framework Integration (MITRE & CVE)
                        mitre_techniques = []
                        for tag in tags:
                            if tag.startswith('attack.t'):
                                tech_id = tag.split('.')[-1].upper()
                                mitre_techniques.append(tech_id)
                                
                        cves = []
                        for tag in tags:
                            if tag.startswith('cve.'):
                                cve_clean = "-".join(tag.split('.')[1:]).upper()
                                cves.append(f"CVE-{cve_clean}")

                        # 4. Final Compilation Append Step
                        compiled_rules.append({
                            "title": title,
                            "severity": severity,
                            "why_it_matters": description,
                            "signature_keywords": clean_keywords,
                            "potential_cves": cves,
                            "mitre_attack": mitre_techniques,
                            "nist_mapping": self._derive_nist(mitre_techniques)
                        })

            except Exception as e:
                # Keep parent process alive if a single file has malformed or abstract syntax
                print(f"[!] Bypassing unreadable rule structure ({filepath.name}): {e}")
                continue

        print(f"[+] Total Active Rules Map Complete: {len(compiled_rules)} signatures successfully compiled into memory.")
        return compiled_rules

    def _derive_nist(self, mitre_techniques):
        """
        Dynamically maps MITRE ATT&CK techniques down to the exact 
        NIST Cyber Security Framework (CSF) v1.1 Subcategory index.
        """
        if not mitre_techniques:
            return {"function": "DETECT", "id": "DE.CM-1", "desc": "Network & host boundaries monitored for anomalies."}
            
        for tech in mitre_techniques:
            # Reconnaissance & Discovery (e.g., T1083, T1018, T1046)
            if tech in ['T1083', 'T1018', 'T1046', 'T1595']:
                return {"function": "DETECT", "id": "DE.AE-2", "desc": "Anomalous events are analyzed to determine potential impact."}
            # Credential Access & Brute Force Operations (e.g., T1110, T1003)
            elif tech in ['T1110', 'T1003', 'T1056']:
                return {"function": "DETECT", "id": "DE.AE-3", "desc": "Incidents are checked against baseline user thresholds."}
            # Execution & Lateral Movement Frameworks (e.g., T1059, T1021)
            elif tech in ['T1059', 'T1021', 'T1204', 'T1566']:
                return {"function": "DETECT", "id": "DE.CM-1", "desc": "Malicious script and command execution streams monitored."}
            # Persistence & Privilege Escalation Hooks (e.g., T1543, T1068)
            elif tech in ['T1543', 'T1068', 'T1078']:
                return {"function": "PROTECT", "id": "PR.AC-4", "desc": "Access permissions and system integrity are managed."}
                
        return {"function": "DETECT", "id": "DE.CM-1", "desc": "Security telemetry events parsed against baseline signatures."}

If your dashboard automatically refreshes or polls an endpoint like /get-alerts on an interval to show live security incidents, search for setInterval or a function name like pollLiveAlerts. Inside that function, you'll find a matching rendering sequence:
JavaScript

function pollLiveAlerts() {
    fetch('/get-alerts')
    .then(res => res.json())
    .then(data => {
        // Look for where alerts are appended to the screen dynamically:
        data.alerts.forEach(alert => {
            // 👈 REPLACE THIS ENTIRE INNER LOOP WITH THE COMPLIANCE BADGE CODE
        });
    });
}

How to place it safely:

Simply erase everything inside that data.alerts.forEach(alert => { ... }) wrapper and drop the updated snippet in. It will immediately begin parsing the new alert.mitre_attack, alert.potential_cves, and alert.nist_mapping JSON properties returned by your upgraded backend.

                    <div>Engine Classification: <span id="meta-engine" style="color: var(--accent-cyan);"></span></div>

                </div>

    <script>
        document.getElementById('upload-form').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            
            const formData = new FormData(this);
            const alertsWrapper = document.getElementById('alerts-wrapper');
            const metaDisplay = document.getElementById('meta-display');
            const aiContainer = document.getElementById('ai-container');
            const aiReportTarget = document.getElementById('ai-report-target');
            
            // Set up processing UI state indicators
            alertsWrapper.innerHTML = `<div class="clean-state" style="color: var(--accent-cyan); border-color: var(--accent-cyan);">[*] Executing pipeline analysis matrices... Parsing rule blocks.</div>`;
            aiContainer.style.display = formData.get('run_ai') === 'true' ? 'block' : 'none';
            aiReportTarget.innerHTML = `<em>Coprocessor spooling up context structures... Please wait.</em>`;
            metaDisplay.style.display = 'none';

            fetch('/analyze-async', {
                method: 'POST',
                body: formData
            })
            .then(response => {
                if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Catastrophic network or parser loop collapse.');
                return response.json();
            })
            .then(data => {
                // Populate Metric Overview Metadata Strip
                document.getElementById('meta-target').innerText = data.filename;
                document.getElementById('meta-engine').innerText = data.log_type;
                document.getElementById('meta-count').innerText = data.alerts.length;
                
                // Colorize the metric counts dynamically based on severity indicators
                document.getElementById('meta-count').style.color = data.alerts.length > 0 ? 'var(--accent-red)' : 'var(--accent-green)';
                metaDisplay.style.display = 'flex';

                // Process AI Report window data elements
                if (data.ai_report) {
                    // Quick conversion helper for basic markdown strings from local models
                    aiReportTarget.innerHTML = data.ai_report
                        .replace(/\n/g, '<br>')
                        .replace(/### (.*?)<br>/g, '<h3 style="margin: 5px 0; color: var(--accent-cyan);">$1</h3>')
                        .replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');
                } else {
                    aiContainer.style.display = 'none';
                }

                // Empty out the dashboard frame wrapper to draw active dynamic cards
                alertsWrapper.innerHTML = '';

                if (data.alerts.length === 0) {
                    alertsWrapper.innerHTML = `
                        <div class="clean-state">
                            [+] Ingestion cycle clean. Context profiles clear of static rule heuristic triggers.
                        </div>`;
                    return;
                }

                // ─── THREAT INTEL BADGE INGESTION MATRIX ───
                data.alerts.forEach(alert => {
                    // 1. Format MITRE ATT&CK Badges
                    let mitreBadges = alert.mitre_attack && alert.mitre_attack.length > 0 
                        ? alert.mitre_attack.map(tech => `<span style="background: #34495e; color: #ecf0f1; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.8em; font-family: monospace; font-weight: bold;">MITRE ${tech}</span>`).join(' ')
                        : `<span style="background: #2c3e50; color: #7f8c8d; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.8em;">No MITRE Tag</span>`;

                    // 2. Format CVE Vulnerability Badges 
                    let cveBadges = alert.potential_cves && alert.potential_cves.length > 0
                        ? alert.potential_cves.map(cve => `<span style="background: #c0392b; color: #fff; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.8em; font-family: monospace; font-weight: bold;">${cve}</span>`).join(' ')
                        : '';

                    // 3. Format NIST Framework Compliance Strip
                    let nistLabel = alert.nist_mapping 
                        ? `<div style="margin-top: 10px; font-size: 0.82em; font-family: monospace; color: var(--accent-cyan);">
                            <strong>NIST CSF Alignment:</strong> 
                            <span style="background: rgba(6, 182, 212, 0.1); padding: 1px 5px; border-radius: 2px; border: 1px solid var(--accent-cyan);">
                                ${alert.nist_mapping.function} // ${alert.nist_mapping.id}
                            </span> 
                            <span style="color: var(--text-muted); margin-left: 4px;">— ${alert.nist_mapping.desc}</span>
                           </div>`
                        : '';

                    const alertDiv = document.createElement('div');
                    alertDiv.className = `alert-item severity-${alert.severity}`;
                    alertDiv.innerHTML = `
                        <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: flex-start; flex-wrap: wrap; gap: 10px;">
                            <h4 style="margin: 0; font-size: 1.1em; color: var(--text-light); letter-spacing: -0.3px;">${alert.title}</h4>
                            <div style="display: flex; gap: 5px; flex-wrap: wrap;">
                                ${cveBadges}
                                ${mitreBadges}
                                <span style="padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.8em; font-weight: bold; background: rgba(255,255,255,0.08);">${alert.severity}</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        
                        <p style="margin: 8px 0 4px 0; font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Culprit Vector Asset:</strong> <code>${alert.source || '127.0.0.1'}</code></p>
                        <p style="margin: 4px 0 8px 0; color: var(--text-muted); font-size: 0.9em; line-height: 1.45;">${alert.why_it_matters}</p>
                        
                        ${nistLabel}
                    `;
                    alertsWrapper.appendChild(alertDiv);
                });
            })
            .catch(err => {
                alertsWrapper.innerHTML = `<div class="clean-state" style="color: var(--accent-red); border-color: var(--accent-red);">[-] Error: ${err.message}</div>`;
                aiContainer.style.display = 'none';
            });
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/chart.js"></script>


<script>

    let livePollingInterval = null;

    let timelineChartInstance = null;

    let severityChartInstance = null;

    let hasChartRenderedData = false;


    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    // ACCORDION TOGGLE MANAGEMENT COMPONENT

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    function toggleVisibilitySection(sectionId, arrowId) {

        const element = document.getElementById(sectionId);

        const arrow = document.getElementById(arrowId);

        

        if (element.style.display === "grid" || element.style.display === "block") {

            element.style.display = "none";

            arrow.innerText = "▶";

        } else {

            // Apply proper layout wrappers on reveal

            element.style.display = (sectionId === "analytics-visualization-row") ? "grid" : "block";

            arrow.innerText = "▼";

        }

    }


    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    // DYNAMIC GRAPHIC RENDERING INFRASTRUCTURE LAYER

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    function renderAnalyticsCharts(alerts) {

        if (!alerts || alerts.length === 0) {

            hasChartRenderedData = false;

            return;

        }

        hasChartRenderedData = true;


        const severityCounts = { CRITICAL: 0, HIGH: 0, MEDIUM: 0, LOW: 0 };

        alerts.forEach(a => {

            if (severityCounts[a.severity] !== undefined) severityCounts[a.severity]++;

        });


        const timeBuckets = {};

        alerts.forEach(a => {

            let timeLabel = "Live Wire Window";

            if (a.timestamp) {

                const dateObj = new Date(a.timestamp * 1000);

                timeLabel = dateObj.toTimeString().split(' ')[0];

            }

            timeBuckets[timeLabel] = (timeBuckets[timeLabel] || 0) + 1;

        });


        const timelineLabels = Object.keys(timeBuckets).sort();

        const timelineData = timelineLabels.map(label => timeBuckets[label]);


        if (timelineChartInstance) timelineChartInstance.destroy();

        if (severityChartInstance) severityChartInstance.destroy();


        const ctxTimeline = document.getElementById('timelineChart').getContext('2d');

        timelineChartInstance = new Chart(ctxTimeline, {

            type: 'line',

            data: {

                labels: timelineLabels.length > 0 ? timelineLabels : ["Capture Stream"],

                datasets: [{

                    label: 'Threat Spikes',

                    data: timelineData.length > 0 ? timelineData : [alerts.length],

                    borderColor: '#00adb5',

                    backgroundColor: 'rgba(0, 173, 181, 0.1)',

                    borderWidth: 2,

                    tension: 0.3,

                    fill: true

                }]

            },

            options: {

                responsive: true,

                maintainAspectRatio: false,

                plugins: { legend: { display: false } },

                scales: {

                    x: { ticks: { color: '#a0a0b0', font: { size: 10 } }, grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)' } },

                    y: { ticks: { color: '#a0a0b0', font: { size: 10 }, stepSize: 1 }, grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)' } }

                }

            }

        });


        const ctxSeverity = document.getElementById('severityChart').getContext('2d');

        severityChartInstance = new Chart(ctxSeverity, {

            type: 'doughnut',

            data: {

                labels: ['Critical', 'High', 'Medium', 'Low'],

                datasets: [{

                    data: [severityCounts.CRITICAL, severityCounts.HIGH, severityCounts.MEDIUM, severityCounts.LOW],

                    backgroundColor: ['#ff5722', '#e67e22', '#f1c40f', '#34495e'],

                    borderWidth: 0

                }]

            },

            options: {

                responsive: true,

                maintainAspectRatio: false,

                plugins: {

                    legend: { position: 'right', labels: { color: '#eeeeee', font: { size: 11 } } }

                }

            }

        });

    }


    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    // LIVE PACKET SNIFFER DASHBOARD CONTROL ENGINE

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    async function toggleLiveCapture(enable) {

        try {

            document.getElementById('upload-form').reset();

            

            const response = await fetch('/live-sniffer/toggle', {

                method: 'POST',

                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },

                body: JSON.stringify({ enable: enable })

            });

            

            document.getElementById('start-live-btn').disabled = enable;

            document.getElementById('stop-live-btn').disabled = !enable;

            const statusText = document.getElementById('live-status-text');

            

            if (enable) {

                statusText.innerText = "Status: ACTIVE & SNIFFING...";

                statusText.style.color = "var(--accent-orange)";

                

                document.getElementById('initial-placeholder').style.display = 'none';

                document.getElementById('results-display').style.display = 'block';

                document.getElementById('res-filename').innerText = "[LIVE WIRE CAPTURE]";

                document.getElementById('res-log-type').innerText = "LIVE_PCAP_SNIFFER";

                document.getElementById('ai-report-wrapper').style.display = 'none';

                

                livePollingInterval = setInterval(pollLiveAlerts, 1500);

            } else {

                statusText.innerText = "Status: PAUSED";

                statusText.style.color = "var(--text-muted)";

                clearInterval(livePollingInterval);

            }

        } catch (err) {

            alert(`Live Engine Socket Failure: ${err.message}`);

        }

    }


    async function pollLiveAlerts() {

        try {

            const response = await fetch('/live-sniffer/alerts');

            const data = await response.json();

            

            const alertsWrapper = document.getElementById('alerts-wrapper');

            document.getElementById('res-alert-count').innerText = data.alerts ? data.alerts.length : 0;


            renderAnalyticsCharts(data.alerts);


            const clearExistingPlaybook = document.getElementById('live-playbook-card');

            if (clearExistingPlaybook) clearExistingPlaybook.remove();

            

            if (data.playbook_compiled) {

                const playbookPanel = document.createElement('div');

                playbookPanel.id = "live-playbook-card";

                playbookPanel.style.background = 'var(--bg-primary)';

                playbookPanel.style.border = '1px dashed var(--accent-orange)';

                playbookPanel.style.padding = '15px';

                playbookPanel.style.borderRadius = '6px';

                playbookPanel.style.marginBottom = '18px';

                playbookPanel.innerHTML = `

                    <h4 style="color: var(--accent-orange); margin: 0 0 8px 0;">📋 Live Mitigation Playbook Hot-Compiled</h4>

                    <p style="margin: 0 0 8px 0; font-size: 0.9em;">Active threats hitting live sockets generated manual terminal remediation sequences.</p>

                    <p style="margin: 0; font-size: 0.85em; color: var(--text-muted);"><strong>Target Path:</strong> <code style="color: var(--accent-orange)">artifacts/live_remediation_playbook.txt</code></p>

                `;

                alertsWrapper.insertBefore(playbookPanel, alertsWrapper.firstChild);

            }


            const activeCards = alertsWrapper.querySelectorAll('.alert-item');

            activeCards.forEach(c => c.remove());


            if (data.alerts && data.alerts.length > 0) {

                data.alerts.forEach(alert => {

                    const alertDiv = document.createElement('div');

                    alertDiv.className = `alert-item severity-${alert.severity}`;

                    alertDiv.innerHTML = `

                        <h4 style="margin: 0 0 8px 0; font-size: 1.05em;">${alert.title} [${alert.severity}]</h4>

                        <p style="margin: 4px 0; font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Live Culprit Node:</strong> <code>${alert.source}</code></p>

                        <p style="margin: 6px 0 0 0; color: var(--text-muted); font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Risk Rationalization:</strong> ${alert.why_it_matters}</p>

                    `;

                    alertsWrapper.appendChild(alertDiv);

                });

            } else {

                const cleanMsg = document.createElement('div');

                cleanMsg.className = "alert-item";

                cleanMsg.style.borderLeftColor = "var(--accent-green)";

                cleanMsg.innerHTML = `<p style="color: var(--accent-green); font-weight: bold; margin:0;">[+] Monitoring socket boundaries. No signatures matched on active wire frames.</p>`;

                alertsWrapper.appendChild(cleanMsg);

            }

        } catch (e) {

            console.error("Error connecting to live server telemetry socket:", e);

        }

    }


    async function clearLiveMetrics() {

        clearInterval(livePollingInterval);

        await fetch('/live-sniffer/clear', { method: 'POST' });

        document.getElementById('alerts-wrapper').innerHTML = '';

        document.getElementById('res-alert-count').innerText = '0';

        document.getElementById('analytics-visualization-row').style.display = 'none';

        document.getElementById('charts-arrow').innerText = "▶";

        if (timelineChartInstance) timelineChartInstance.destroy();

        if (severityChartInstance) severityChartInstance.destroy();

        toggleLiveCapture(false);

    }


    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    // HISTORICAL FILE INGESTION PIPELINE MANAGEMENT

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    document.getElementById('upload-form').addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {

        e.preventDefault();

        

        if (livePollingInterval) toggleLiveCapture(false);


        const fileInput = document.getElementById('file-input');

        const overrideSelect = document.getElementById('override-select');

        const aiCheckbox = document.getElementById('ai-checkbox');

        const submitBtn = document.getElementById('submit-btn');

        const progressContainer = document.getElementById('progress-container');

        const progressFill = document.getElementById('progress-fill');

        const statusMessage = document.getElementById('status-message');

        

        const placeholder = document.getElementById('initial-placeholder');

        const resultsDisplay = document.getElementById('results-display');

        const alertsWrapper = document.getElementById('alerts-wrapper');

        const aiReportWrapper = document.getElementById('ai-report-wrapper');


        if (!fileInput.files.length) return;


        submitBtn.disabled = true;

        placeholder.style.display = 'none';

        resultsDisplay.style.display = 'block';

        alertsWrapper.innerHTML = '';

        aiReportWrapper.style.display = 'none';

        

        // Hide charts on new upload until completed

        document.getElementById('analytics-visualization-row').style.display = 'none';

        document.getElementById('charts-arrow').innerText = "▶";


        progressContainer.style.display = 'block';

        progressFill.style.width = '10%';

        statusMessage.innerText = "Initializing file ingestion pipeline...";


        const formData = new FormData();

        formData.append('file', fileInput.files[0]);

        formData.append('override_type', overrideSelect.value);

        formData.append('run_ai', aiCheckbox.checked);


        let progress = 10;

        const progressInterval = setInterval(() => {

            if (progress < 85) {

                progress += Math.floor(Math.random() * 8) + 3;

                if (progress > 85) progress = 85;

                progressFill.style.width = `${progress}%`;

                

                if (progress < 35) {

                    statusMessage.innerText = "Applying data structure parsing models...";

                } else if (progress < 65) {

                    statusMessage.innerText = "Executing pluggable cross-protocol signature matrices...";

                } else {

                    statusMessage.innerText = aiCheckbox.checked ? 

                        "Local AI model engaged. Evaluating payload indicators (takes a moment)..." : 

                        "Finalizing analytical telemetry data...";

                }

            }

        }, 400);


        try {

            const response = await fetch('/analyze-async', {

                method: 'POST',

                body: formData

            });

            

            clearInterval(progressInterval);

            if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`Pipeline HTTP status breakage: ${response.status}`);


            const data = await response.json();


            progressFill.style.width = '100%';

            statusMessage.innerText = "Analysis matrix completed.";


            document.getElementById('res-filename').innerText = data.filename;

            document.getElementById('res-log-type').innerText = data.log_type;

            document.getElementById('res-alert-count').innerText = data.alerts ? data.alerts.length : 0;


            // Silently compile chart indices in background

            renderAnalyticsCharts(data.alerts);


            // 1. BOUNDARY CHECK: Parser Override Failures

            if (data.mismatch_detected && (!data.alerts || data.alerts.length === 0) && (!data.ai_report || data.ai_report.includes("Ingestion stream empty"))) {

                alertsWrapper.innerHTML = `

                    <div style="border: 2px dashed #ff5722; background: rgba(255, 87, 34, 0.1); padding: 20px; border-radius: 6px; margin: 15px 0;">

                        <h4 style="color: #ff5722; margin: 0 0 8px 0; font-size: 1.15em;">❌ Ingestion Blocked: Total Parser Incompatibility</h4>

                        <p style="margin: 4px 0; line-height: 1.5;">

                            You forced execution routing to the <code style="background: #0f1015; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 4px; color: #ff5722;">${data.log_type}</code> engine.<br>

                            Because this file actually contains <code style="background: #0f1015; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 4px; color: #00adb5;">${data.auto_detect_type}</code> syntax, the selected parser could not normalize a single line of data.

                        </p>

                    </div>`;

                aiReportWrapper.style.display = 'none';

            } 

            else {

                // 2. CASE: Manual Playbook Compilation

                if (data.playbook_meta && data.playbook_meta.file_created) {

                    const playbookPanel = document.createElement('div');

                    playbookPanel.style.background = 'var(--bg-primary)';

                    playbookPanel.style.border = '1px dashed var(--accent-cyan)';

                    playbookPanel.style.padding = '15px';

                    playbookPanel.style.borderRadius = '6px';

                    playbookPanel.style.marginBottom = '18px';

                    

                    playbookPanel.innerHTML = `

                        <h4 style="color: var(--accent-cyan); margin: 0 0 8px 0; display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 6px;">

                            📋 On-Demand Remediation Playbook Compiled

                        </h4>

                        <p style="margin: 0 0 10px 0; font-size: 0.9em; color: var(--text-light);">

                            SentinelLite has formulated an explicit security mitigation script file containing <strong>${data.playbook_meta.actionable_targets}</strong> actionable infrastructure targets.

                        </p>

                        <p style="margin: 0; font-size: 0.85em; color: var(--text-muted);">

                            <strong>Local Storage Artifact Path:</strong> <code style="color: var(--accent-cyan); background: var(--bg-dark); padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 4px;">${data.playbook_meta.output_path}</code>

                        </p>

                    `;

                    alertsWrapper.appendChild(playbookPanel);

                }


                // 3. CASE: Standard Warnings

                if (data.mismatch_detected) {

                    const warnDiv = document.createElement('div');

                    warnDiv.style.border = '1px dashed var(--accent-orange)';

                    warnDiv.style.background = 'rgba(255, 87, 34, 0.05)';

                    warnDiv.style.padding = '12px';

                    warnDiv.style.borderRadius = '4px';

                    warnDiv.style.marginBottom = '15px';

                    warnDiv.style.fontSize = '0.9em';

                    warnDiv.innerHTML = `⚠ <strong>Structural Boundary Override Mismatch:</strong> Forced <code>${data.log_type}</code> parser but identified file as <code>${data.auto_detect_type}</code>.`;

                    alertsWrapper.appendChild(warnDiv);

                }


                // Render Signature Alerts

                if (data.alerts && data.alerts.length > 0) {

                    data.alerts.forEach(alert => {

                        const alertDiv = document.createElement('div');

                        alertDiv.className = `alert-item severity-${alert.severity}`;

                        alertDiv.innerHTML = `

                            <h4 style="margin: 0 0 8px 0; font-size: 1.05em;">${alert.title} [${alert.severity}]</h4>

                            <p style="margin: 4px 0; font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Culprit Actor Anchor:</strong> <code>${alert.source}</code></p>

                            <p style="margin: 6px 0 0 0; color: var(--text-muted); font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Risk Rationalization:</strong> ${alert.why_it_matters}</p>

                        `;

                        alertsWrapper.appendChild(alertDiv);

                    });

                } else {

                    alertsWrapper.innerHTML += `

                        <div class="alert-item" style="border-left-color: var(--accent-green); background: rgba(78, 159, 61, 0.05)">

                            <p style="color: var(--accent-green); font-weight: bold; margin: 0; font-size: 0.9em;">

                                [+] Ingestion cycle clean. Context profiles clear of static rule heuristic triggers.

                            </p>

                        </div>`;

                }


                // Append local AI Coprocessor response metrics

                if (aiCheckbox.checked && data.ai_report && !data.ai_report.includes("Ingestion stream empty")) {

                    let formattedText = data.ai_report

<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/chart.js"></script>

<script>
    let livePollingInterval = null;
    let timelineChartInstance = null;
    let severityChartInstance = null;
    let hasChartRenderedData = false;

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // ACCORDION TOGGLE MANAGEMENT COMPONENT
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    function toggleVisibilitySection(sectionId, arrowId) {
        const element = document.getElementById(sectionId);
        const arrow = document.getElementById(arrowId);
        
        if (element.style.display === "grid" || element.style.display === "block") {
            element.style.display = "none";
            arrow.innerText = "▶";
        } else {
            element.style.display = (sectionId === "analytics-visualization-row") ? "grid" : "block";
            arrow.innerText = "▼";
        }
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // DYNAMIC GRAPHIC RENDERING INFRASTRUCTURE LAYER
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    function renderAnalyticsCharts(alerts) {
        if (!alerts || alerts.length === 0) {
            hasChartRenderedData = false;
            return;
        }
        hasChartRenderedData = true;

        const severityCounts = { CRITICAL: 0, HIGH: 0, MEDIUM: 0, LOW: 0 };
        alerts.forEach(a => {
            if (severityCounts[a.severity] !== undefined) severityCounts[a.severity]++;
        });

        const timeBuckets = {};
        alerts.forEach(a => {
            let timeLabel = "Live Wire Window";
            if (a.timestamp) {
                const dateObj = new Date(a.timestamp * 1000);
                timeLabel = dateObj.toTimeString().split(' ')[0];
            }
            timeBuckets[timeLabel] = (timeBuckets[timeLabel] || 0) + 1;
        });

        const timelineLabels = Object.keys(timeBuckets).sort();
        const timelineData = timelineLabels.map(label => timeBuckets[label]);

        if (timelineChartInstance) timelineChartInstance.destroy();
        if (severityChartInstance) severityChartInstance.destroy();

        const ctxTimeline = document.getElementById('timelineChart').getContext('2d');
        timelineChartInstance = new Chart(ctxTimeline, {
            type: 'line',
            data: {
                labels: timelineLabels.length > 0 ? timelineLabels : ["Capture Stream"],
                datasets: [{
                    label: 'Threat Spikes',
                    data: timelineData.length > 0 ? timelineData : [alerts.length],
                    borderColor: '#00adb5',
                    backgroundColor: 'rgba(0, 173, 181, 0.1)',
                    borderWidth: 2,
                    tension: 0.3,
                    fill: true
                }]
            },
            options: {
                responsive: true,
                maintainAspectRatio: false,
                plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
                scales: {
                    x: { ticks: { color: '#a0a0b0', font: { size: 10 } }, grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)' } },
                    y: { ticks: { color: '#a0a0b0', font: { size: 10 }, stepSize: 1 }, grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)' } }
                }
            }
        });

        const ctxSeverity = document.getElementById('severityChart').getContext('2d');
        severityChartInstance = new Chart(ctxSeverity, {
            type: 'doughnut',
            data: {
                labels: ['Critical', 'High', 'Medium', 'Low'],
                datasets: [{
                    data: [severityCounts.CRITICAL, severityCounts.HIGH, severityCounts.MEDIUM, severityCounts.LOW],
                    backgroundColor: ['#ff5722', '#e67e22', '#f1c40f', '#34495e'],
                    borderWidth: 0
                }]
            },
            options: {
                responsive: true,
                maintainAspectRatio: false,
                plugins: {
                    legend: { position: 'right', labels: { color: '#eeeeee', font: { size: 11 } } }
                }
            }
        });
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // HELPER FUNCTION: INJECTS COMPLIANCE BADGES INTO ALERT CARD LAYOUT
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    function generateAlertTemplateHTML(alert) {
        // 1. Format MITRE Badges safely
        let mitreBadges = alert.mitre_attack && alert.mitre_attack.length > 0 
            ? alert.mitre_attack.map(tech => `<span style="background: #2c3e50; color: #00adb5; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.8em; font-family: monospace; font-weight: bold; border: 1px solid rgba(0,173,181,0.2);">MITRE ${tech}</span>`).join(' ')
            : `<span style="background: #1a1c23; color: #7f8c8d; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.8em; border: 1px dashed #393e46;">No MITRE Tag</span>`;

        // 2. Format CVE Badges safely
        let cveBadges = alert.potential_cves && alert.potential_cves.length > 0
            ? alert.potential_cves.map(cve => `<span style="background: rgba(255,87,34,0.1); color: #ff5722; padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.8em; font-family: monospace; font-weight: bold; border: 1px solid rgba(255,87,34,0.3);">${cve}</span>`).join(' ')
            : '';

        // 3. Format NIST Framework Matrix Strip layout block
        let nistLabel = alert.nist_mapping 
            ? `<div style="margin-top: 10px; font-size: 0.82em; font-family: monospace; color: var(--accent-cyan); border-top: 1px dashed rgba(255,255,255,0.05); padding-top: 8px;">
                <strong>NIST CSF Alignment:</strong> 
                <span style="background: rgba(0, 173, 181, 0.1); padding: 1px 5px; border-radius: 2px; border: 1px solid var(--accent-cyan); font-weight: bold;">
                    ${alert.nist_mapping.function} // ${alert.nist_mapping.id}
                </span> 
                <span style="color: var(--text-muted); margin-left: 4px;">— ${alert.nist_mapping.desc}</span>
               </div>`
            : '';

        return `
            <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: flex-start; flex-wrap: wrap; gap: 10px;">
                <h4 style="margin: 0; font-size: 1.05em; color: var(--text-light); font-weight: bold;">${alert.title}</h4>
                <div style="display: flex; gap: 6px; flex-wrap: wrap;">
                    ${cveBadges}
                    ${mitreBadges}
                    <span style="padding: 2px 6px; border-radius: 3px; font-size: 0.8em; font-weight: bold; background: rgba(255,255,255,0.08); color: var(--text-light); font-family: monospace;">[${alert.severity}]</span>
                </div>
            </div>
            <p style="margin: 8px 0 4px 0; font-size: 0.9em;"><strong>Culprit Actor Anchor:</strong> <code>${alert.source || '127.0.0.1'}</code></p>
            <p style="margin: 4px 0 8px 0; color: var(--text-muted); font-size: 0.9em; line-height: 1.45;"><strong>Risk Rationalization:</strong> ${alert.why_it_matters}</p>
            ${nistLabel}
        `;
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // LIVE PACKET SNIFFER DASHBOARD CONTROL ENGINE
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    async function toggleLiveCapture(enable) {
        try {
            document.getElementById('upload-form').reset();
            
            const response = await fetch('/live-sniffer/toggle', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ enable: enable })
            });
            
            document.getElementById('start-live-btn').disabled = enable;
            document.getElementById('stop-live-btn').disabled = !enable;
            const statusText = document.getElementById('live-status-text');
            
            if (enable) {
                statusText.innerText = "Status: ACTIVE & SNIFFING...";
                statusText.style.color = "var(--accent-orange)";
                
                document.getElementById('initial-placeholder').style.display = 'none';
                document.getElementById('results-display').style.display = 'block';
                document.getElementById('res-filename').innerText = "[LIVE WIRE CAPTURE]";
                document.getElementById('res-log-type').innerText = "LIVE_PCAP_SNIFFER";
                document.getElementById('ai-report-wrapper').style.display = 'none';
                
                livePollingInterval = setInterval(pollLiveAlerts, 1500);
            } else {
                statusText.innerText = "Status: PAUSED";
                statusText.style.color = "var(--text-muted)";
                clearInterval(livePollingInterval);
            }
        } catch (err) {
            alert(`Live Engine Socket Failure: ${err.message}`);
        }
    }

    async function pollLiveAlerts() {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/live-sniffer/alerts');
            const data = await response.json();
            
            const alertsWrapper = document.getElementById('alerts-wrapper');
            document.getElementById('res-alert-count').innerText = data.alerts ? data.alerts.length : 0;

            renderAnalyticsCharts(data.alerts);

            const clearExistingPlaybook = document.getElementById('live-playbook-card');
            if (clearExistingPlaybook) clearExistingPlaybook.remove();
            
            if (data.playbook_compiled) {
                const playbookPanel = document.createElement('div');
                playbookPanel.id = "live-playbook-card";
                playbookPanel.style.background = 'var(--bg-primary)';
                playbookPanel.style.border = '1px dashed var(--accent-orange)';
                playbookPanel.style.padding = '15px';
                playbookPanel.style.borderRadius = '6px';
                playbookPanel.style.marginBottom = '18px';
                playbookPanel.innerHTML = `
                    <h4 style="color: var(--accent-orange); margin: 0 0 8px 0;">📋 Live Mitigation Playbook Hot-Compiled</h4>
                    <p style="margin: 0 0 8px 0; font-size: 0.9em;">Active threats hitting live sockets generated manual terminal remediation sequences.</p>
                    <p style="margin: 0; font-size: 0.85em; color: var(--text-muted);"><strong>Target Path:</strong> <code style="color: var(--accent-orange)">artifacts/live_remediation_playbook.txt</code></p>
                `;
                alertsWrapper.insertBefore(playbookPanel, alertsWrapper.firstChild);
            }

            const activeCards = alertsWrapper.querySelectorAll('.alert-item');
            activeCards.forEach(c => c.remove());

            if (data.alerts && data.alerts.length > 0) {
                data.alerts.forEach(alert => {
                    const alertDiv = document.createElement('div');
                    alertDiv.className = `alert-item severity-${alert.severity}`;
                    alertDiv.innerHTML = generateAlertTemplateHTML(alert);
                    alertsWrapper.appendChild(alertDiv);
                });
            } else {
                const cleanMsg = document.createElement('div');
                cleanMsg.className = "alert-item";
                cleanMsg.style.borderLeftColor = "var(--accent-green)";
                cleanMsg.innerHTML = `<p style="color: var(--accent-green); font-weight: bold; margin:0; font-size: 0.9em;">[+] Monitoring socket boundaries. No signatures matched on active wire frames.</p>`;
                alertsWrapper.appendChild(cleanMsg);
            }
        } catch (e) {
            console.error("Error connecting to live server telemetry socket:", e);
        }
    }

    async function clearLiveMetrics() {
        clearInterval(livePollingInterval);
        await fetch('/live-sniffer/clear', { method: 'POST' });
        document.getElementById('alerts-wrapper').innerHTML = '';
        document.getElementById('res-alert-count').innerText = '0';
        document.getElementById('analytics-visualization-row').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('charts-arrow').innerText = "▶";
        if (timelineChartInstance) timelineChartInstance.destroy();
        if (severityChartInstance) severityChartInstance.destroy();
        toggleLiveCapture(false);
    }

    document.getElementById('upload-form').addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
